-- LATEST_FIXED_2026_06_29: notification, scrollbar, waypoint text, and input layout fixes applied.
-- Services
local TweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")
local UserInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService")
local CoreGui = game:GetService("CoreGui")
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
local HttpService = game:GetService("HttpService")

local Player = Players.LocalPlayer
local InterfaceScale = 1.18

local KeybindStorageFile = "HqydeuLoader_Keybinds.json"
local SavedKeybinds = {}
local CanPersistKeybinds = type(isfile) == "function" and type(readfile) == "function" and type(writefile) == "function"
if type(getgenv) == "function" then
	local globalSettings = getgenv().HqydeuLoader_Settings
	if type(globalSettings) == "table" then SavedKeybinds = globalSettings end
end

if CanPersistKeybinds then
	pcall(function()
		if isfile(KeybindStorageFile) then
			local decoded = HttpService:JSONDecode(readfile(KeybindStorageFile))
			if type(decoded) == "table" then SavedKeybinds = decoded end
		end
	end)
end
if type(getgenv) == "function" then
	local globalSettings = getgenv().HqydeuLoader_Settings
	if type(globalSettings) == "table" then SavedKeybinds = globalSettings end
end

local GuiSizeValue = math.clamp(tonumber(SavedKeybinds.GuiSize) or 50, 20, 100)
local function GuiScaleFromValue(value)
	return InterfaceScale * (value / 50)
end

local function LoadKeybind(featureName)
	local savedName = SavedKeybinds[featureName]
	if type(savedName) == "string" then
		local success, keyCode = pcall(function() return Enum.KeyCode[savedName] end)
		if success and keyCode then return keyCode end
	end
	return Enum.KeyCode.Unknown
end

local function SavePersistentSettings()
	if type(getgenv) == "function" then
		getgenv().HqydeuLoader_Settings = SavedKeybinds
	end
	if CanPersistKeybinds then
		pcall(function() writefile(KeybindStorageFile, HttpService:JSONEncode(SavedKeybinds)) end)
	end
end

local function SaveKeybind(featureName, keyCode)
	SavedKeybinds[featureName] = keyCode.Name
	SavePersistentSettings()
end

local function LoadColor(settingName, fallback)
	local saved = SavedKeybinds[settingName]
	if type(saved) == "table" and tonumber(saved.R) and tonumber(saved.G) and tonumber(saved.B) then
		return Color3.fromRGB(saved.R, saved.G, saved.B)
	end
	return fallback
end

local function PackColor(color)
	return {
		R = math.floor(color.R * 255 + 0.5),
		G = math.floor(color.G * 255 + 0.5),
		B = math.floor(color.B * 255 + 0.5),
	}
end

local function UnpackColor(saved, fallback)
	if type(saved) == "table" and tonumber(saved.R) and tonumber(saved.G) and tonumber(saved.B) then
		return Color3.fromRGB(saved.R, saved.G, saved.B)
	end
	return fallback
end

local DefaultFrameColor = Color3.fromRGB(28, 28, 38)
local DefaultAccentColor = Color3.fromRGB(0, 210, 255)
local FrameThemeColor = DefaultFrameColor
local AccentColor = LoadColor("ThemeAccent", DefaultAccentColor)

local function SaveThemeColors()
	SavedKeybinds.ThemeFrame = nil
	SavedKeybinds.ThemeAccent = PackColor(AccentColor)
	SavePersistentSettings()
end

local function KeybindText(keyCode)
	return keyCode == Enum.KeyCode.Unknown and "..." or keyCode.Name
end

-- Theme Management
local ThemeObjects = { Backgrounds = {}, Texts = {}, Accents = {}, AccentBackgrounds = {}, StateTexts = {} }
local HubState = {}
ThemeObjects.FeatureKeybindEntries = {}
ThemeObjects.AddFeatureKeybind = function(entry)
	if type(entry) ~= "table" or type(entry.Name) ~= "string" or type(entry.Get) ~= "function" or type(entry.Set) ~= "function" then return end
	table.insert(ThemeObjects.FeatureKeybindEntries, entry)
	if entry.Parent and entry.Toggle and ThemeObjects.AttachFeatureKeybindButton then
		ThemeObjects.AttachFeatureKeybindButton(entry, entry.Parent, entry.Toggle)
	end
	if entry.Button and ThemeObjects.AttachKeybindClearPrompt then
		if ThemeObjects.EnsureKeybindOutline then ThemeObjects.EnsureKeybindOutline(entry.Button) end
		ThemeObjects.AttachKeybindClearPrompt(entry, entry.Button)
	end
	if ThemeObjects.RefreshKeybindEditor then ThemeObjects.RefreshKeybindEditor() end
end

ThemeObjects.BeginFeatureKeybind = function(entry, button)
	if type(entry) ~= "table" or type(entry.Set) ~= "function" then return end
	PlayClick()
	if ThemeObjects.KeybindEditorConnection then
		ThemeObjects.KeybindEditorConnection:Disconnect()
		ThemeObjects.KeybindEditorConnection = nil
	end
	HubState.IsBindingKeybindEditor = true
	if button then button.Text = "..." end
	ThemeObjects.KeybindEditorConnection = UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, processed)
		if processed then return end
		if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Keyboard then
			local selectedKey = input.KeyCode
			if selectedKey == Enum.KeyCode.Backspace or selectedKey == Enum.KeyCode.Delete then
				selectedKey = Enum.KeyCode.Unknown
			end
			entry.Set(selectedKey)
			if entry.InlineButton then entry.InlineButton.Text = KeybindText(selectedKey) end
			HubState.IsBindingKeybindEditor = false
			if ThemeObjects.KeybindEditorConnection then
				ThemeObjects.KeybindEditorConnection:Disconnect()
				ThemeObjects.KeybindEditorConnection = nil
			end
			if ThemeObjects.RefreshKeybindEditor then ThemeObjects.RefreshKeybindEditor() end
		end
	end)
end

ThemeObjects.ShowKeybindClearPrompt = function(entry, button)
	if type(entry) ~= "table" or type(entry.Set) ~= "function" or not button then return end
	if ThemeObjects.KeybindClearPrompt then ThemeObjects.KeybindClearPrompt:Destroy() end
	local prompt = Instance.new("Frame")
	prompt.Name = "KeybindClearPrompt"
	prompt.Size = UDim2.new(0, 150, 0, 64)
	prompt.Position = UDim2.fromOffset(button.AbsolutePosition.X, button.AbsolutePosition.Y + button.AbsoluteSize.Y + 4)
	prompt.BackgroundColor3 = FrameThemeColor
	prompt.BackgroundTransparency = 0.04
	prompt.BorderSizePixel = 0
	prompt.ZIndex = 230
	prompt.Parent = ScreenGui
	ThemeObjects.KeybindClearPrompt = prompt
	Instance.new("UICorner", prompt).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 8)
	local stroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
	stroke.Name = "ControlOutline"
	stroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
	stroke.Thickness = 1
	stroke.Transparency = 0
	stroke.Parent = prompt

	local label = Instance.new("TextLabel")
	label.Size = UDim2.new(1, -12, 0, 28)
	label.Position = UDim2.new(0, 6, 0, 5)
	label.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	label.Text = "Remove keybind?"
	label.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
	label.TextSize = 10
	label.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
	label.TextStrokeColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
	label.TextStrokeTransparency = 0.5
	label.ZIndex = 231
	label.Parent = prompt

	local yes = Instance.new("TextButton")
	yes.Size = UDim2.new(0, 58, 0, 20)
	yes.Position = UDim2.new(0, 16, 0, 38)
	yes.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 35, 35)
	yes.BorderSizePixel = 0
	yes.Text = "Yes"
	yes.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
	yes.TextSize = 9
	yes.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
	yes.ZIndex = 231
	yes.Parent = prompt
	Instance.new("UICorner", yes).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 5)

	local no = Instance.new("TextButton")
	no.Size = UDim2.new(0, 58, 0, 20)
	no.Position = UDim2.new(0, 78, 0, 38)
	no.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(45, 45, 45)
	no.BorderSizePixel = 0
	no.Text = "No"
	no.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
	no.TextSize = 9
	no.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
	no.ZIndex = 231
	no.Parent = prompt
	Instance.new("UICorner", no).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 5)

	yes.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		PlayClick()
		entry.Set(Enum.KeyCode.Unknown)
		if entry.InlineButton then entry.InlineButton.Text = "..." end
		if button and button.Parent then button.Text = "..." end
		if ThemeObjects.RefreshKeybindEditor then ThemeObjects.RefreshKeybindEditor() end
		if ThemeObjects.KeybindClearPrompt then ThemeObjects.KeybindClearPrompt:Destroy(); ThemeObjects.KeybindClearPrompt = nil end
	end)
	no.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		PlayClick()
		if ThemeObjects.KeybindClearPrompt then ThemeObjects.KeybindClearPrompt:Destroy(); ThemeObjects.KeybindClearPrompt = nil end
	end)
end

ThemeObjects.AttachKeybindClearPrompt = function(entry, button)
	if not button or not button.MouseButton2Click or button:GetAttribute("KeybindClearAttached") then return end
	button:SetAttribute("KeybindClearAttached", true)
	button.MouseButton2Click:Connect(function()
		PlayClick()
		ThemeObjects.ShowKeybindClearPrompt(entry, button)
	end)
end

ThemeObjects.AttachFeatureKeybindButton = function(entry, parent, toggle)
	if not parent or not parent:IsA("GuiObject") or entry.InlineButton then return end
	if toggle and toggle:IsA("GuiObject") then
		toggle.Size = UDim2.new(0, 44, 0, 22)
		toggle.Position = UDim2.new(1, -98, 0, 8)
		toggle.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(45, 45, 45)
		toggle.BackgroundTransparency = 0.8
		toggle.TextSize = 9
	end
	local button = Instance.new("TextButton")
	button.Name = "FeatureKeybindButton"
	button.Size = UDim2.new(0, 44, 0, 22)
	button.Position = UDim2.new(1, -50, 0, 8)
	button.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(45, 45, 45)
	button.BackgroundTransparency = 0.8
	button.BorderSizePixel = 0
	button.Text = KeybindText(entry.Get())
	button.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
	button.TextSize = 8
	button.TextColor3 = AccentColor
	button.Parent = parent
	table.insert(ThemeObjects.Backgrounds, button)
	table.insert(ThemeObjects.Accents, button)
	Instance.new("UICorner", button).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 5)
	local stroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
	stroke.Name = "ControlOutline"
	stroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
	stroke.Thickness = 1
	stroke.Transparency = 0
	stroke.Parent = button
	entry.InlineButton = button
	button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		ThemeObjects.BeginFeatureKeybind(entry, button)
	end)
	ThemeObjects.AttachKeybindClearPrompt(entry, button)
end

HubState.NotificationSound.Parent = HubState.NotificationHolder

HubState.ToggleOnSound.Volume = 0.55

HubState.ToggleOffSound = Instance.new("Sound")

HubState.ToggleOffSound.Parent = MainFrame

ThemeObjects.ApplyMainGradient = function(intensity)
	intensity = math.clamp(intensity or 0.5, 0, 1)
	local bgColor = FrameThemeColor
	MainTextureGradient.Color = ColorSequence.new({
		ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0, bgColor:Lerp(AccentColor, intensity * 0.16)),
		ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0.14, bgColor:Lerp(AccentColor, intensity * 0.74)),
		ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0.46, bgColor:Lerp(AccentColor, intensity)),
		ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0.72, bgColor:Lerp(AccentColor, intensity * 0.98)),
		ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(1, bgColor:Lerp(AccentColor, intensity * 0.62)),
	})
	if TargetTextureGradient then TargetTextureGradient.Color = MainTextureGradient.Color end
	if ThemeObjects.PlayerTP and ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.Gradient then ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.Gradient.Color = MainTextureGradient.Color end
	if ThemeObjects.KeybindEditorGradient then ThemeObjects.KeybindEditorGradient.Color = MainTextureGradient.Color end
end

local function IsFrameLight()
	return (FrameThemeColor.R * 0.299 + FrameThemeColor.G * 0.587 + FrameThemeColor.B * 0.114) > 0.58
end

local function InactiveTextColor()
	return Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
end

ThemeObjects.IsStateTextObject = function(target)
	for _, entry in ipairs(ThemeObjects.StateTexts) do
		if entry.Object == target then return true end
	end
	return false
end

ThemeObjects.IsMenuTextObject = function(target)
	return (ThemeObjects.PlayerTP and ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.Frame and target:IsDescendantOf(ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.Frame))
		or (ThemeObjects.WaypointUI and ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.Frame and target:IsDescendantOf(ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.Frame))
end

ThemeObjects.RefreshScrollBars = function(root)
	for _, object in ipairs((root or ScreenGui):GetDescendants()) do
		if object:IsA("ScrollingFrame") then
			object.ScrollBarImageColor3 = AccentColor
		end
	end
end

ThemeObjects.LayoutNotifications = function()
	for index, item in ipairs(HubState.Notifications) do
		if item.Frame and item.Frame.Parent then
			TweenService:Create(item.Frame, TweenInfo.new(0.2, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {
				Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, (index - 1) * 28),
			}):Play()
		end
	end
end

ThemeObjects.RemoveNotification = function(item)
	if item.Removing then return end
	item.Removing = true
	for index = #HubState.Notifications, 1, -1 do
		if HubState.Notifications[index] == item then
			table.remove(HubState.Notifications, index)
			break
		end
	end
	ThemeObjects.LayoutNotifications()
	if item.Stroke then
		TweenService:Create(item.Stroke, TweenInfo.new(0.18, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.In), {Transparency = 1}):Play()
	end
	if item.Label then
		TweenService:Create(item.Label, TweenInfo.new(0.18, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.In), {TextTransparency = 1, TextStrokeTransparency = 1}):Play()
	end
	if item.Frame then
		TweenService:Create(item.Frame, TweenInfo.new(0.18, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.In), {BackgroundTransparency = 1}):Play()
		task.delay(0.2, function()
			if item.Frame then item.Frame:Destroy() end
		end)
	end
end

ThemeObjects.ShowNotification = function(message)
	if not HubState.NotificationHolder or not HubState.NotificationHolder.Parent then return end
	if not HubState.NotificationSound.IsPlaying then
		HubState.NotificationSound.TimePosition = 0
		HubState.NotificationSound:Play()
	end
	local item = {}
	item.Frame = Instance.new("Frame")
	item.Frame.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 24)
	item.Frame.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 28)
	item.Frame.BackgroundColor3 = FrameThemeColor
	item.Frame.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	item.Frame.BorderSizePixel = 0
	item.Frame.ZIndex = 201
	item.Frame.Parent = HubState.NotificationHolder
	Instance.new("UICorner", item.Frame).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 5)
	item.Stroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
	item.Stroke.Color = AccentColor
	item.Stroke.Thickness = 1.4
	item.Stroke.Transparency = 1
	item.Stroke.Parent = item.Frame
	item.Label = Instance.new("TextLabel")
	item.Label.Size = UDim2.new(1, -20, 1, 0)
	item.Label.Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, 0)
	item.Label.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	item.Label.Text = tostring(message)
	item.Label.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
	item.Label.TextSize = 11
	item.Label.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
	item.Label.TextStrokeColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
	item.Label.TextStrokeTransparency = 1
	item.Label.TextTransparency = 1
	item.Label.TextTruncate = Enum.TextTruncate.AtEnd
	item.Label.ZIndex = 202
	item.Label.Parent = item.Frame
	table.insert(HubState.Notifications, item)
	while #HubState.Notifications > 2 do
		ThemeObjects.RemoveNotification(HubState.Notifications[1])
	end
	ThemeObjects.LayoutNotifications()
	TweenService:Create(item.Frame, TweenInfo.new(0.18, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {BackgroundTransparency = 0.08}):Play()
	TweenService:Create(item.Stroke, TweenInfo.new(0.18, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {Transparency = 0.2}):Play()
	TweenService:Create(item.Label, TweenInfo.new(0.18, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {TextTransparency = 0, TextStrokeTransparency = 0.55}):Play()
	task.delay(2.1, function()
		ThemeObjects.RemoveNotification(item)
	end)
end

ThemeObjects.RefreshStateTexts = function(instant)
	local tweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(instant and 0 or 0.2, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.Out)
	for i = #ThemeObjects.StateTexts, 1, -1 do
		local entry = ThemeObjects.StateTexts[i]
		if entry.Object and entry.Object.Parent then
			local success, enabled = pcall(entry.IsEnabled)
			enabled = success and enabled == true
			local featureName = tostring(entry.Name or entry.Object.Text or "Feature")
			featureName = featureName:gsub("<[^>]->", "")
			featureName = featureName:gsub("%s*:%s*[Oo]n%s*$", "")
			featureName = featureName:gsub("%s*:%s*[Oo]ff%s*$", "")
			featureName = featureName:gsub("%s*:%s*$", "")
			if entry.LastEnabled ~= nil and enabled ~= entry.LastEnabled then
				local toggleSound = enabled and HubState.ToggleOnSound or HubState.ToggleOffSound
				if toggleSound then
					toggleSound:Stop()
					toggleSound.TimePosition = 0
					toggleSound:Play()
				end
				ThemeObjects.ShowNotification(featureName .. (enabled and " enabled" or " disabled"))
			elseif enabled and entry.LastEnabled == nil then
				ThemeObjects.ShowNotification(featureName .. " enabled")
			end
			entry.LastEnabled = enabled
			local stateColor = enabled and AccentColor or InactiveTextColor()
			local currentColor = entry.Object.TextColor3
			local needsColorUpdate = math.abs(currentColor.R - stateColor.R) > 0.004
				or math.abs(currentColor.G - stateColor.G) > 0.004
				or math.abs(currentColor.B - stateColor.B) > 0.004
			if needsColorUpdate then
				if instant then
					entry.Object.TextColor3 = stateColor
				else
					TweenService:Create(entry.Object, tweenInfo, {TextColor3 = stateColor}):Play()
				end
			end
		else
			table.remove(ThemeObjects.StateTexts, i)
		end
	end
end

ThemeObjects.StyleTextOutline = function(obj)
	if obj:IsA("TextLabel") or obj:IsA("TextButton") or obj:IsA("TextBox") then
		obj.TextStrokeColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
		obj.TextTransparency = 0
		obj.TextStrokeTransparency = obj == SplashText and 1 or 0.5
	end
end

ThemeObjects.RefreshToggleButton = function(obj)
	if not obj:IsA("TextButton") or (obj.Text ~= "On" and obj.Text ~= "Off") then return end
	local baseColor = obj.Text == "On" and AccentColor or FrameThemeColor:Lerp(Color3.new(0, 0, 0), 0.22)
	local baseTransparency = obj.Text == "On" and 0 or 0.8
	if obj:GetAttribute("ButtonHovered") then
		baseColor = baseColor:Lerp(AccentColor, obj.Text == "On" and 0.24 or 0.42)
		baseTransparency = math.max(0, baseTransparency - 0.32)
	end
	obj.BackgroundColor3 = baseColor
	obj.BackgroundTransparency = baseTransparency
	obj.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
end

ThemeObjects.ApplyHoveredButtonStyle = function(obj)
	if not obj:IsA("TextButton") then return end
	local hoverColor = obj.BackgroundColor3:Lerp(AccentColor, obj.Text == "On" and 0.24 or 0.42)
	local hoverTransparency = math.max(0, obj.BackgroundTransparency - 0.32)
	obj.BackgroundColor3 = hoverColor
	obj.BackgroundTransparency = hoverTransparency
end

ThemeObjects.ApplyRestingButtonStyle = function(obj)
	if not obj:IsA("TextButton") then return end
	local bgColor = FrameThemeColor
	local secBgColor = bgColor:Lerp(Color3.new(0, 0, 0), 0.22)
	local keepSolid = obj.Name == "DestroyBtn" or obj.Name == "ResetCharacterBtn" or obj.Name == "RejoinBtn"
		or obj.Name == "ServerHopBtn" or obj.Name == "GuiSizeBtn" or obj.Name == "ClearKeybindsBtn"
		or obj.Name == "EditKeybindsBtn"
	local target = secBgColor
	local targetTransparency = (keepSolid or obj.Text == "On") and 0 or 0.8
	if obj.Name == "MM2GameButton" or obj.Name == "QuietOrDieGameButton" then
		target = Color3.fromRGB(65, 65, 67)
		targetTransparency = 0.92
	elseif obj.Name == "ESPColorBtn" then
		target = HubState.ESPColor
		targetTransparency = 0
	elseif obj.Name:find("SavedColorSlot", 1, true) then
		target = obj.BackgroundColor3
		targetTransparency = obj.Text == "+" and 0.8 or 0.15
	elseif obj.Text == "On" then
		target = AccentColor
	end
	if obj.Name == "DestroyBtn" then target = Color3.fromRGB(255, 35, 35)
	elseif obj.Name == "ResetCharacterBtn" then target = Color3.fromRGB(255, 230, 0)
	elseif obj.Name == "RejoinBtn" then target = Color3.fromRGB(0, 230, 255)
	elseif obj.Name == "ServerHopBtn" then target = Color3.fromRGB(0, 105, 255)
	elseif obj.Name == "GuiSizeBtn" then target = Color3.fromRGB(70, 255, 70)
	elseif obj.Name == "ClearKeybindsBtn" then target = Color3.fromRGB(195, 35, 255)
	elseif obj.Name == "EditKeybindsBtn" then target = Color3.fromRGB(255, 130, 35) end
	obj.BackgroundColor3 = target
	obj.BackgroundTransparency = targetTransparency
end

ThemeObjects.StyleControlOutline = function(obj)
	if not obj:IsA("GuiObject") then return end
	if obj:FindFirstChild("ControlOutline") then return end
	local isVisibleButton = obj:IsA("TextButton") and obj.BackgroundTransparency < 0.9
	local isVisibleInput = obj:IsA("TextBox") and obj.BackgroundTransparency < 0.9
	local isTile = obj:IsA("Frame") and (obj.Name:find("Card", 1, true) or obj.Name:find("Row", 1, true))
	local isScrollBackdrop = obj:IsA("ScrollingFrame") and obj.BackgroundTransparency < 1
	local parentName = obj.Parent and obj.Parent.Name or ""
	local isListItem = obj:IsA("Frame") and (parentName == "PlayerScroll" or parentName == "TargetScroll"
		or parentName == "WaypointScroll" or parentName == "WaypointList" or parentName == "WaypointsList")
	if not isVisibleButton and not isVisibleInput and not isTile and not isScrollBackdrop and not isListItem then return end
	local outline = Instance.new("UIStroke")
	outline.Name = "ControlOutline"
	outline.ApplyStrokeMode = Enum.ApplyStrokeMode.Border
	outline.Color = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
	outline.Thickness = 1
	outline.Transparency = 0.18
	outline.Parent = obj
end

ThemeObjects.EnsureKeybindOutline = function(button)
	if not button or not button:IsA("GuiObject") then return end
	local outline = button:FindFirstChild("ControlOutline")
	if not outline then
		outline = Instance.new("UIStroke")
		outline.Name = "ControlOutline"
		outline.ApplyStrokeMode = Enum.ApplyStrokeMode.Border
		outline.Parent = button
	end
	outline.Color = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
	outline.Thickness = 1
	outline.Transparency = 0
end

ThemeObjects.AttachHoverSound = function(obj)
	if not obj:IsA("TextButton") or obj:GetAttribute("HoverSoundAttached") then return end
	if obj.BackgroundTransparency >= 0.98 and obj.Text == "" then return end
	obj:SetAttribute("HoverSoundAttached", true)
	obj.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
		PlayHover()
		obj:SetAttribute("ButtonHovered", true)
		obj:SetAttribute("HoverBaseTransparency", obj.BackgroundTransparency)
		obj:SetAttribute("HoverBaseR", obj.BackgroundColor3.R)
		obj:SetAttribute("HoverBaseG", obj.BackgroundColor3.G)
		obj:SetAttribute("HoverBaseB", obj.BackgroundColor3.B)
		ThemeObjects.ApplyHoveredButtonStyle(obj)
		local outline = obj:FindFirstChild("ControlOutline")
		if outline and outline:IsA("UIStroke") then
			outline:SetAttribute("HoverBaseThickness", outline.Thickness)
			outline:SetAttribute("HoverBaseTransparency", outline.Transparency)
			outline.Thickness = math.max(outline.Thickness, 1.8)
			outline.Transparency = 0
		end
	end)
	obj.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
		obj:SetAttribute("ButtonHovered", false)
		local baseR = obj:GetAttribute("HoverBaseR")
		local baseG = obj:GetAttribute("HoverBaseG")
		local baseB = obj:GetAttribute("HoverBaseB")
		local baseTransparency = obj:GetAttribute("HoverBaseTransparency")
		if baseR and baseG and baseB and baseTransparency then
			obj.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(baseR, baseG, baseB)
			obj.BackgroundTransparency = baseTransparency
		else
			ThemeObjects.ApplyRestingButtonStyle(obj)
		end
		local outline = obj:FindFirstChild("ControlOutline")
		if outline and outline:IsA("UIStroke") then
			local baseThickness = outline:GetAttribute("HoverBaseThickness")
			local baseStrokeTransparency = outline:GetAttribute("HoverBaseTransparency")
			if baseThickness and baseStrokeTransparency then
				outline.Thickness = baseThickness
				outline.Transparency = baseStrokeTransparency
			end
		end
	end)
end

ThemeObjects.NormalizeMainTileWidth = function(obj)
	if not obj:IsA("GuiObject") or not obj:IsDescendantOf(MainFrame) then return end
	local name = obj.Name or ""
	local parentName = obj.Parent and obj.Parent.Name or ""
	if parentName == "PlayerScroll" or parentName == "TargetScroll" or parentName == "WaypointScroll"
		or parentName == "WaypointList" or parentName == "WaypointsList" then return end
	local isFeatureTile = obj:IsA("Frame") and (name:find("Row", 1, true) or name:find("Card", 1, true))
	local isGameTile = obj:IsA("TextButton") and (name == "MM2GameButton" or name == "QuietOrDieGameButton")
	if not isFeatureTile and not isGameTile then return end
	local size = obj.Size
	local position = obj.Position
	obj.Size = UDim2.new(1, -24, size.Y.Scale, size.Y.Offset)
	obj.Position = UDim2.new(0, 12, position.Y.Scale, position.Y.Offset)
	ThemeObjects.StyleControlOutline(obj)
end

local function CompactGuiText(root)
	for _, obj in ipairs(root:GetDescendants()) do
		ThemeObjects.NormalizeMainTileWidth(obj)
		ThemeObjects.AttachHoverSound(obj)
		ThemeObjects.StyleTextOutline(obj)
		ThemeObjects.StyleControlOutline(obj)
		local isMainContent = obj:IsDescendantOf(MainFrame)
		if isMainContent and obj:IsA("TextButton") and (obj.Name == "MM2GameButton" or obj.Name == "QuietOrDieGameButton") then
			obj.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
			obj.TextSize = 11
			obj.TextWrapped = false
			obj.TextStrokeColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
			obj.TextStrokeTransparency = 0.5
		elseif isMainContent and (obj:IsA("TextButton") or obj:IsA("TextBox")) then
			obj.TextSize = math.min(obj.TextSize, 12)
			obj.TextWrapped = true
			obj.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
			obj.TextTransparency = 0
			if obj:IsA("TextBox") then
				obj.PlaceholderColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
				obj.TextStrokeColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
				obj.TextStrokeTransparency = 0.5
			end
		elseif isMainContent and obj:IsA("TextLabel") and obj.TextSize > 13 then
			obj.TextSize = 13
		end
	end
end

local function UpdateTheme(instant)
	local bgColor = FrameThemeColor
	local lightTheme = IsFrameLight()
	local secBgColor = bgColor:Lerp(Color3.new(0, 0, 0), 0.22)
	local textColor = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
	local subTextColor = InactiveTextColor()
	local tweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(instant and 0 or 0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.Out)
	
	TweenService:Create(MainFrame, tweenInfo, {BackgroundColor3 = bgColor}):Play()
	if SplashFrame and SplashFrame.Parent then SplashFrame.BackgroundColor3 = bgColor end
	ThemeObjects.ApplyMainGradient(0.5)
	MainTextureStroke.Color = AccentColor
	ThemeObjects.RefreshScrollBars(ScreenGui)
	for _, line in ipairs(MainPatternLines) do
		if line.Parent then line.BackgroundColor3 = AccentColor end
	end
	for i = #ThemeObjects.Backgrounds, 1, -1 do
		local obj = ThemeObjects.Backgrounds[i]
		if obj.Parent then
			ThemeObjects.NormalizeMainTileWidth(obj)
			ThemeObjects.AttachHoverSound(obj)
			if (obj:IsA("TextButton") or obj:IsA("TextBox")) then
				local keepSolid = obj.Name == "DestroyBtn" or obj.Name == "ResetCharacterBtn" or obj.Name == "RejoinBtn"
					or obj.Name == "ServerHopBtn" or obj.Name == "GuiSizeBtn" or obj.Name == "ClearKeybindsBtn"
					or obj.Name == "EditKeybindsBtn"
				if obj.Name == "MM2GameButton" or obj.Name == "QuietOrDieGameButton" then
					obj.BackgroundTransparency = 0.92
				elseif obj.Name == "ESPColorBtn" then
					obj.BackgroundTransparency = 0
				elseif obj.Name:find("SavedColorSlot", 1, true) then
					obj.BackgroundTransparency = obj.Text == "+" and 0.8 or 0.15
				else
					obj.BackgroundTransparency = (keepSolid or obj.Text == "On") and 0 or 0.8
				end
			end
		local target = (obj:IsA("TextButton") or obj:IsA("TextBox") or obj.Name == "TabScroll" or obj.Name == "TargetRow") and secBgColor or bgColor
			local targetTransparency = obj.BackgroundTransparency
			if obj.Name == "PlayerTPFrame" then target = Color3.fromRGB(14, 18, 26)
			end
			if obj.Name == "MM2GameButton" or obj.Name == "QuietOrDieGameButton" then target = Color3.fromRGB(65, 65, 67) end
			if obj.Name == "ESPColorBtn" then target = HubState.ESPColor end
			if obj.Name:find("SavedColorSlot", 1, true) then target = obj.BackgroundColor3 end
			if obj:IsA("TextButton") and obj.Text == "On" then target = AccentColor end
			if obj.Name == "DestroyBtn" then target = Color3.fromRGB(255, 35, 35)
			elseif obj.Name == "ResetCharacterBtn" then target = Color3.fromRGB(255, 230, 0)
			elseif obj.Name == "RejoinBtn" then target = Color3.fromRGB(0, 230, 255)
			elseif obj.Name == "ServerHopBtn" then target = Color3.fromRGB(0, 105, 255)
			elseif obj.Name == "GuiSizeBtn" then target = Color3.fromRGB(70, 255, 70)
			elseif obj.Name == "ClearKeybindsBtn" then target = Color3.fromRGB(195, 35, 255)
			elseif obj.Name == "EditKeybindsBtn" then target = Color3.fromRGB(255, 130, 35) end
			if obj:IsA("TextButton") and obj:GetAttribute("ButtonHovered") then
				target = target:Lerp(AccentColor, obj.Text == "On" and 0.24 or 0.42)
				obj.BackgroundTransparency = math.max(0, targetTransparency - 0.32)
			end
			TweenService:Create(obj, tweenInfo, {BackgroundColor3 = target}):Play()
		else
			table.remove(ThemeObjects.Backgrounds, i)
		end
	end
	for i = #ThemeObjects.Texts, 1, -1 do
		local obj = ThemeObjects.Texts[i]
		if obj.Parent then
			if not ThemeObjects.IsStateTextObject(obj) then
				local parentName = obj.Parent and obj.Parent.Name or ""
				local isTileTitle = obj:IsA("TextLabel") and (parentName:find("Card", 1, true) or parentName:find("Row", 1, true))
				local isToggleText = obj:IsA("TextButton") and (obj.Text == "On" or obj.Text == "Off")
				local target = (obj.Name == "NavTabButton" and (obj.Text == ThemeObjects.ActiveTabName or (obj == HubState.GamesTabButton and ThemeObjects.ActiveTabName == "Games"))) and AccentColor or Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
				TweenService:Create(obj, tweenInfo, {TextColor3 = target}):Play()
			end
		else
			table.remove(ThemeObjects.Texts, i)
		end
	end
	for i = #ThemeObjects.Accents, 1, -1 do
		local obj = ThemeObjects.Accents[i]
		if obj.Parent then
			if obj:IsA("UIStroke") then obj.Color = AccentColor
			elseif obj:IsA("GuiObject") then obj.TextColor3 = AccentColor end
		else
			table.remove(ThemeObjects.Accents, i)
		end
	end
	for i = #ThemeObjects.AccentBackgrounds, 1, -1 do
		local obj = ThemeObjects.AccentBackgrounds[i]
		if obj.Parent then
			TweenService:Create(obj, tweenInfo, {BackgroundColor3 = AccentColor}):Play()
			if obj:IsA("TextButton") then
				obj.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
			end
		else
			table.remove(ThemeObjects.AccentBackgrounds, i)
		end
	end
	ThemeObjects.RefreshStateTexts(instant)
end
ThemeObjects.UpdateTheme = UpdateTheme

HubState.Connections = {}
local function TrackConnection(name, connection)
	if HubState.Connections[name] then
		HubState.Connections[name]:Disconnect()
	end
	HubState.Connections[name] = connection
	return connection
end
HubState.Connections.TextOutline = ScreenGui.DescendantAdded:Connect(function(object)
	ThemeObjects.StyleTextOutline(object)
	ThemeObjects.StyleControlOutline(object)
end)
ThemeObjects.GradientPulseTime = 0
ThemeObjects.GradientPulseAccumulator = 0
ThemeObjects.ToggleColorAccumulator = 0
ThemeObjects.UprightCFrame = function(sourceCFrame, position)
	local _, yaw = sourceCFrame:ToOrientation()
	return CFrame.new(position or sourceCFrame.Position) * CFrame.Angles(0, yaw, 0)
end
ThemeObjects.SetRootUpright = function(root, sourceCFrame, position)
	if not root then return end
	root.CFrame = ThemeObjects.UprightCFrame(sourceCFrame or root.CFrame, position or root.Position)
	root.AssemblyAngularVelocity = Vector3.zero
end
HubState.Connections.GradientPulse = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function(deltaTime)
	if not MainFrame.Visible then return end
	ThemeObjects.GradientPulseTime = ThemeObjects.GradientPulseTime + deltaTime
	ThemeObjects.GradientPulseAccumulator = ThemeObjects.GradientPulseAccumulator + deltaTime
	ThemeObjects.ToggleColorAccumulator = ThemeObjects.ToggleColorAccumulator + deltaTime
	if ThemeObjects.ToggleColorAccumulator >= 0.25 then
		ThemeObjects.ToggleColorAccumulator = 0
		ThemeObjects.RefreshStateTexts(true)
	end
	if ThemeObjects.GradientPulseAccumulator < 0.033 then return end
	ThemeObjects.GradientPulseAccumulator = 0
	if type(ThemeObjects.ApplyMainGradient) == "function" then
		local pulse = 0.5 + ((math.sin(ThemeObjects.GradientPulseTime * 1.35) + 1) * 0.25)
		pcall(ThemeObjects.ApplyMainGradient, pulse)
	end
end)
ThemeObjects.FreeCam = {Enabled = false, Keybind = LoadKeybind("FreeCam"), Binding = false}

ThemeObjects.UpdateEmblemPosition = function()
	if not MainPatternLines.Container then return end
	MainPatternLines.Container.Visible = false
end

ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature = {Enabled = false, Applying = false, Lighting = game:GetService("Lighting")}
ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Page = Instance.new("Frame")
ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Page.Name = "ExtrasPage"
ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Page.Size = UDim2.new(0, 346, 1, -54)
ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Page.Position = UDim2.new(1.1, 0, 0, 54)
ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Page.BackgroundTransparency = 1
ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Page.BorderSizePixel = 0
ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Page.ClipsDescendants = true
ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Page.Visible = false
ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Page.Parent = MainFrame
ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Original = {
	Brightness = ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Lighting.Brightness,
	ClockTime = ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Lighting.ClockTime,
	FogEnd = ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Lighting.FogEnd,
	GlobalShadows = ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Lighting.GlobalShadows,
	Ambient = ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Lighting.Ambient,
	OutdoorAmbient = ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Lighting.OutdoorAmbient,
	ExposureCompensation = ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Lighting.ExposureCompensation,
}
function ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Apply()
	if not ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Enabled or ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Applying then return end
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Applying = true
	pcall(function()
		ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Lighting.Brightness = 3
		ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Lighting.ClockTime = 14
		ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Lighting.FogEnd = 100000
		ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Lighting.GlobalShadows = false
		ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Lighting.Ambient = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
		ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Lighting.OutdoorAmbient = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
		ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Lighting.ExposureCompensation = 0.35
	end)
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Applying = false
end
function ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Restore()
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Enabled = false
	for property, value in pairs(ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Original) do
		pcall(function() ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Lighting[property] = value end)
	end
end

function ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.BuildPath(instance)
	if not instance then return "" end
	local nodes = {}
	local current = instance
	while current and current.Parent and current.Parent ~= game do
		table.insert(nodes, 1, current)
		current = current.Parent
	end
	if not current or current.Parent ~= game then return instance:GetFullName() end
	local function escapeName(name) return tostring(name):gsub("\\", "\\\\"):gsub('"', '\\"') end
	local path = 'game:GetService("' .. escapeName(current.Name) .. '")'
	for _, node in ipairs(nodes) do
		if node.Name:match("^[%a_][%w_]*$") then path = path .. "." .. node.Name
		else path = path .. '["' .. escapeName(node.Name) .. '"]' end
	end
	return path
end

function ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.BeginSelection(purpose)
	if ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.CopyFrame.Visible then PlaySwoosh() end
	if ThemeObjects.PickerDock then ThemeObjects.PickerDock.Visible = false end
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.SelectionPurpose = purpose or "Copy"
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Selecting = true
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.SelectStarted = os.clock()
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.SelectedPart = nil
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.PartToggle.Text = "On"
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.PartTitle.TextColor3 = AccentColor
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.CopyFrame.Visible = false
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.CopyButton.Visible = false
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.WaypointButton.Visible = false
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.CopyStatus.Text = ""
	if ThemeObjects.WaypointUI and ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.AddButton then ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.AddButton.Text = "Cancel Selection" end
end

function ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.EndSelection(hidePopup)
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Selecting = false
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.PartToggle.Text = "Off"
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.PartTitle.TextColor3 = InactiveTextColor()
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.HoverHighlight.Enabled = false
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.HoverHighlight.Adornee = nil
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.SelectionBox.Visible = false
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.SelectionBox.Adornee = nil
	if hidePopup and ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.CopyFrame.Visible then
		ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.CopyFrame.Visible = false
		PlaySwoosh()
	end
	if ThemeObjects.WaypointUI and ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.AddButton then ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.AddButton.Text = "Select Part" end
end

ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.PartToggle.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
	PlayClick()
	if ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Selecting then ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.EndSelection(true)
	else ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.BeginSelection("Copy") end
end)

HubState.Connections.ExtrasPartHover = RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
	if not ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Selecting then return end
	local target = ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Mouse.Target
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.HoverHighlight.OutlineColor = AccentColor
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.HoverHighlight.Adornee = target
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.HoverHighlight.Enabled = target ~= nil and target:IsA("BasePart")
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.SelectionBox.Color3 = AccentColor
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.SelectionBox.Adornee = target and target:IsA("BasePart") and target or nil
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.SelectionBox.Visible = target ~= nil and target:IsA("BasePart")
end)

HubState.Connections.ExtrasPartClick = UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, processed)
	if processed or input.UserInputType ~= Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then return end
	if not ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Selecting or os.clock() - (ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.SelectStarted or 0) < 0.2 then return end
	local target = ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Mouse.Target
	if not target or not target:IsA("BasePart") then return end
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.SelectedPart = target
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Selecting = false
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.PartToggle.Text = "Off"
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.PartTitle.TextColor3 = InactiveTextColor()
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.HoverHighlight.Adornee = target
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.HoverHighlight.Enabled = true
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.SelectionBox.Color3 = AccentColor
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.SelectionBox.Adornee = target
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.SelectionBox.Visible = true
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.SelectedText.Text = "Selected: " .. target.Name
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.CopyStatus.Text = ""
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.CopyButton.Visible = ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.SelectionPurpose == "Copy"
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.WaypointButton.Visible = ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.SelectionPurpose == "Waypoint"
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.CopyFrame.Visible = true
	PlaySwoosh()
	if ThemeObjects.WaypointUI and ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.AddButton then ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.AddButton.Text = "Select Part" end
end)

ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.CopyButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
	PlayClick()
	local selectedPart = ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.SelectedPart
	if not selectedPart or not selectedPart.Parent then return end
	local path = ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.BuildPath(selectedPart)
	local copyFunction = type(setclipboard) == "function" and setclipboard or (type(toclipboard) == "function" and toclipboard or nil)
	if copyFunction and pcall(copyFunction, path) then
		ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.CopyStatus.Text = "Copied to clipboard"
		ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.CopyStatus.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(125, 255, 75)
	else
		ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.CopyStatus.Text = "Clipboard unavailable"
		ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.CopyStatus.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 110, 110)
	end
	task.delay(0.35, function() ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.EndSelection(true) end)
end)

ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.WaypointButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
	PlayClick()
	local selectedPart = ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.SelectedPart
	if not selectedPart or not selectedPart.Parent then return end
	if ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.AddWaypoint then
		ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.AddWaypoint(selectedPart)
		ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.CopyStatus.Text = "Waypoint added"
		ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.CopyStatus.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(125, 255, 75)
	else
		ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.CopyStatus.Text = "Waypoint panel unavailable"
		ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.CopyStatus.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 110, 110)
	end
	task.delay(0.35, function() ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.EndSelection(true) end)
end)

ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.DeselectButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
	PlayClick()
	local purpose = ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.SelectionPurpose
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.SelectedPart = nil
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.EndSelection(true)
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.BeginSelection(purpose)
end)

ThemeObjects.CleanupPartSelector = function()
	if ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.HoverHighlight then ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.HoverHighlight:Destroy() end
	if ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.SelectionBox then ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.SelectionBox:Destroy() end
end
HubState.Connections.FullBright = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
	if not ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Enabled then return end
	if os.clock() - (ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.LastApply or 0) < 0.5 then return end
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.LastApply = os.clock()
	ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Apply()
end)
ThemeObjects.RestoreFullBright = ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Restore

	local function FormatWholeNumber(value)
		local formatted = tostring(math.floor(tonumber(value) or 0))
		while true do
			local replacements
			formatted, replacements = formatted:gsub("^(-?%d+)(%d%d%d)", "%1,%2")
			if replacements == 0 then break end
		end
		return formatted
	end
	local function FormatCompactNumber(value)
		value = math.max(0, math.floor(tonumber(value) or 0))
		local divisor, suffix = 1, ""
		if value >= 1000000000 then divisor, suffix = 1000000000, "B"
		elseif value >= 1000000 then divisor, suffix = 1000000, "M"
		elseif value >= 1000 then divisor, suffix = 1000, "K"
		else return tostring(value) end
		local scaled = value / divisor
		local formatted = scaled >= 100 and string.format("%.0f", scaled) or string.format("%.1f", scaled)
		formatted = formatted:gsub("%.0$", "")
		return formatted .. suffix
	end

	local executionHistory = type(SavedKeybinds.QODOnlyExecutionHistory) == "table" and SavedKeybinds.QODOnlyExecutionHistory or {}
	farmState.AllTime = type(SavedKeybinds.QODAllTimeStats) == "table" and SavedKeybinds.QODAllTimeStats or {Coins = 0, Wins = 0, BestCoins = 0, BestWins = 0}
	farmState.AllTime.Coins = tonumber(farmState.AllTime.Coins) or 0
	farmState.AllTime.Wins = tonumber(farmState.AllTime.Wins) or 0
	farmState.AllTime.BestCoins = tonumber(farmState.AllTime.BestCoins) or 0
	farmState.AllTime.BestWins = tonumber(farmState.AllTime.BestWins) or 0
	if type(SavedKeybinds.QODAllTimeStats) ~= "table" then
		for _, entry in ipairs(executionHistory) do
			farmState.AllTime.Coins = farmState.AllTime.Coins + (tonumber(entry.Coins) or 0)
			farmState.AllTime.Wins = farmState.AllTime.Wins + (tonumber(entry.Wins) or 0)
			if (tonumber(entry.Coins) or 0) > farmState.AllTime.BestCoins
				or ((tonumber(entry.Coins) or 0) == farmState.AllTime.BestCoins and (tonumber(entry.Wins) or 0) > farmState.AllTime.BestWins) then
				farmState.AllTime.BestCoins = tonumber(entry.Coins) or 0
				farmState.AllTime.BestWins = tonumber(entry.Wins) or 0
			end
		end
	end
	local currentExecution = nil
	SavedKeybinds.QODOnlyExecutionHistory = executionHistory
	SavedKeybinds.QODAllTimeStats = farmState.AllTime
	SavePersistentSettings()

	local function RefreshExecutionHistory()
		local lines = {}
		local bestEntry = executionHistory[1] or {Coins = 0, Wins = 0}
		for _, entry in ipairs(executionHistory) do
			local entryCoins = tonumber(entry.Coins) or 0
			local bestCoins = tonumber(bestEntry.Coins) or 0
			local entryWins = tonumber(entry.Wins) or 0
			local bestWins = tonumber(bestEntry.Wins) or 0
			if entryCoins > bestCoins or (entryCoins == bestCoins and entryWins > bestWins) then
				bestEntry = entry
			end
		end
		bestEntry = {Coins = farmState.AllTime.BestCoins, Wins = farmState.AllTime.BestWins}
		historyBest.Text = string.format("Best  •  +%s Coins  •  +%s Wins", FormatCompactNumber(bestEntry.Coins or 0), FormatCompactNumber(bestEntry.Wins or 0))
		for index, entry in ipairs(executionHistory) do
			local useNumber = #executionHistory - index + 1
			table.insert(lines, string.format("%d.  +%s Coins   •   +%s Wins", useNumber, FormatCompactNumber(entry.Coins or 0), FormatCompactNumber(entry.Wins or 0)))
		end
		historyText.Text = table.concat(lines, "\n")
		historyPanel.TotalLabel.Text = string.format('Total  <font color="#7DFF4B">%s Coins</font>  |  <font color="#FFDC41">%s Wins</font>', FormatCompactNumber(farmState.AllTime.Coins), FormatCompactNumber(farmState.AllTime.Wins))
	end
	RefreshExecutionHistory()
	ThemeObjects.FlushQuietHistory = function()
		if not coinsDisplayState.HistoryDirty then return end
		SavedKeybinds.QODOnlyExecutionHistory = executionHistory
		SavedKeybinds.QODAllTimeStats = farmState.AllTime
		SavePersistentSettings()
		coinsDisplayState.HistoryDirty = false
		coinsDisplayState.LastHistorySave = os.clock()
	end
	historyButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		PlayClick()
		historyPanel.Visible = not historyPanel.Visible
		if historyPanel.Visible then RefreshExecutionHistory() end
	end)

	HubState.Connections.QuietOrDieCoinsDisplay = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
		if os.clock() - coinsDisplayState.LastUpdate < 0.2 then return end
		coinsDisplayState.LastUpdate = os.clock()
		local replicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
		local playerGui = Player:FindFirstChildOfClass("PlayerGui")
		local isQuietOrDie = replicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("AbilityEvent") ~= nil
			and playerGui ~= nil and playerGui:FindFirstChild("InGameGui") ~= nil
		if not isQuietOrDie then
			coinsDisplay.Text = "Coins: N/A"
			sessionProfitDisplay.Text = "N/A"
			winsDisplay.Text = "Wins: N/A"
			winsGainDisplay.Text = "N/A"
			return
		end
		if not currentExecution then
			currentExecution = {Coins = 0, Wins = 0, Game = "QuietOrDie"}
			table.insert(executionHistory, 1, currentExecution)
			while #executionHistory > 5 do table.remove(executionHistory) end
			SavedKeybinds.QODOnlyExecutionHistory = executionHistory
			SavePersistentSettings()
			RefreshExecutionHistory()
		end
		local leaderstats = Player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
		local coins = leaderstats and leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Coins")
		local wins = leaderstats and leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Wins")
		coinsDisplay.Text = coins and ("Coins: " .. FormatWholeNumber(coins.Value)) or "Coins: N/A"
		if coins then
			local currentCoins = math.floor(tonumber(coins.Value) or 0)
			if farmState.LastCoins ~= nil and currentCoins > farmState.LastCoins then
				local earnedCoins = currentCoins - farmState.LastCoins
				farmState.ExecutionGain = farmState.ExecutionGain + earnedCoins
				farmState.AllTime.Coins = farmState.AllTime.Coins + earnedCoins
			end
			farmState.LastCoins = currentCoins
		end
		sessionProfitDisplay.Text = coins and ("+" .. FormatCompactNumber(farmState.ExecutionGain)) or "N/A"
		winsDisplay.Text = wins and ("Wins: " .. FormatWholeNumber(wins.Value)) or "Wins: N/A"
		if wins then
			local currentWins = math.floor(tonumber(wins.Value) or 0)
			if farmState.LastWins ~= nil and currentWins > farmState.LastWins then
				local earnedWins = currentWins - farmState.LastWins
				farmState.ExecutionWins = farmState.ExecutionWins + earnedWins
				farmState.AllTime.Wins = farmState.AllTime.Wins + earnedWins
			end
			farmState.LastWins = currentWins
		end
		winsGainDisplay.Text = wins and ("+" .. FormatCompactNumber(farmState.ExecutionWins)) or "N/A"
		if currentExecution.Coins ~= farmState.ExecutionGain or currentExecution.Wins ~= farmState.ExecutionWins then
			currentExecution.Coins = farmState.ExecutionGain
			currentExecution.Wins = farmState.ExecutionWins
			if currentExecution.Coins > farmState.AllTime.BestCoins
				or (currentExecution.Coins == farmState.AllTime.BestCoins and currentExecution.Wins > farmState.AllTime.BestWins) then
				farmState.AllTime.BestCoins = currentExecution.Coins
				farmState.AllTime.BestWins = currentExecution.Wins
			end
			coinsDisplayState.HistoryDirty = true
			if historyPanel.Visible then RefreshExecutionHistory() end
		end
		if coinsDisplayState.HistoryDirty and os.clock() - coinsDisplayState.LastHistorySave >= 5 then
			ThemeObjects.FlushQuietHistory()
		end
	end)

	end)

	end})

	table.insert(ThemeObjects.StateTexts, {Object = reviveTitle, IsEnabled = function() return reviveState.Enabled end})

		reviveToggle.Text = reviveState.Enabled and "On" or "Off"

	ThemeObjects.AddFeatureKeybind({Name = "Auto Farm", Storage = "QODAutoFarm", Parent = farmRow, Toggle = farmToggle, Get = function() return LoadKeybind("QODAutoFarm") end, Set = function(key) SaveKeybind("QODAutoFarm", key) end, Action = function()
		farmState.Enabled = not farmState.Enabled
		if farmState.Enabled and eventState.Enabled and farmState.SafePlace then

			eventTitle.TextColor3 = InactiveTextColor()

		farmState.DroppedCharacter = nil

		farmToggle.Text = farmState.Enabled and "On" or "Off"
		farmTitle.TextColor3 = farmState.Enabled and AccentColor or InactiveTextColor()
	end})

	local function IsQuietOrDieSurvivor()
		local playerGui = Player:FindFirstChildOfClass("PlayerGui")
		local inGameGui = playerGui and playerGui:FindFirstChild("InGameGui")
		local playerFrame = inGameGui and inGameGui:FindFirstChild("PlayerFrameGame")
		local survivorVisible = playerFrame ~= nil and playerFrame.Visible and Player:FindFirstChild("InHit") == nil
		if not survivorVisible then
			farmState.SurvivorSince = 0
			return false
		end
		if farmState.SurvivorSince == 0 then
			farmState.SurvivorSince = os.clock()
			return false
		end
		return os.clock() - farmState.SurvivorSince >= 0.75
	end

	local function IsQuietOrDieKiller()
		local killerFolder = workspace:FindFirstChild("KillerFolder")
		if killerFolder and killerFolder:FindFirstChild(Player.Name) then return true end
		local function containerSaysKiller(container)
			if not container then return false end
			for _, attributeName in ipairs({"Role", "CurrentRole", "RoundRole"}) do
				local value = container:GetAttribute(attributeName)
				if type(value) == "string" and value:lower():find("killer", 1, true) then return true end
			end
			for _, attributeName in ipairs({"IsKiller", "Killer"}) do
				if container:GetAttribute(attributeName) == true then return true end
			end
			for _, valueName in ipairs({"Role", "CurrentRole", "RoundRole"}) do
				local valueObject = container:FindFirstChild(valueName)
				if valueObject and valueObject:IsA("StringValue") and valueObject.Value:lower():find("killer", 1, true) then return true end
			end
			for _, valueName in ipairs({"IsKiller", "Killer"}) do
				local valueObject = container:FindFirstChild(valueName)
				if valueObject and valueObject:IsA("BoolValue") and valueObject.Value then return true end
			end
			return false
		end

		if containerSaysKiller(Player) or containerSaysKiller(Player.Character) then return true end
		if Player.Team and Player.Team.Name:lower():find("killer", 1, true) then return true end
		local playerGui = Player:FindFirstChildOfClass("PlayerGui")
		local inGameGui = playerGui and playerGui:FindFirstChild("InGameGui")
		if inGameGui then
			for _, frameName in ipairs({"KillerFrameGame2", "KillerFrameGame", "KillerFrame", "KillerGui"}) do
				local frame = inGameGui:FindFirstChild(frameName, true)
				if frame and frame:IsA("GuiObject") and frame.Visible then return true end
			end
		end
		return false
	end

	HubState.Connections.QuietOrDieAutoReveal = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
		if not ThemeObjects.QODReveal.Enabled then return end
		if ThemeObjects.QODReveal.LastFire ~= 0 and os.clock() - ThemeObjects.QODReveal.LastFire < 0.5 then return end
		local playerGui = Player:FindFirstChildOfClass("PlayerGui")
		local inGameGui = playerGui and playerGui:FindFirstChild("InGameGui")
		local killerFrame = inGameGui and inGameGui:FindFirstChild("KillerFrameGame2")
		if killerFrame and killerFrame.Visible then
			pcall(function()
				local virtualInput = game:GetService("VirtualInputManager")
				virtualInput:SendKeyEvent(true, Enum.KeyCode.E, false, game)
				task.delay(0.03, function()
					pcall(function() virtualInput:SendKeyEvent(false, Enum.KeyCode.E, false, game) end)
				end)
			end)
		end
		local abilityEvent = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("AbilityEvent")
		if not abilityEvent or not abilityEvent:IsA("RemoteEvent") then return end
		if pcall(function() abilityEvent:FireServer(3) end) then
			ThemeObjects.QODReveal.LastFire = os.clock()
		end
	end)

	HubState.Connections.QuietOrDieAutoRevive = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
		if not reviveState.Enabled or os.clock() - reviveState.LastCheck < 0.03 then return end
		reviveState.LastCheck = os.clock()
		local playersFolder = workspace:FindFirstChild("PlayersFolder")
		local character = Player.Character
		local humanoid = character and character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
		local root = character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
		if not playersFolder or not humanoid or humanoid.Health <= 0 or not root then return end

		local now = os.clock()
		for prompt, lastTriggered in pairs(reviveState.Triggered) do
			if not prompt.Parent or now - lastTriggered > 2 then reviveState.Triggered[prompt] = nil end
		end
		for _, targetCharacter in ipairs(playersFolder:GetChildren()) do
			if targetCharacter ~= character and targetCharacter:IsA("Model") then
				local targetRoot = targetCharacter and targetCharacter:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
				local attachment = targetRoot and targetRoot:FindFirstChild("ReviveAttachment")
					or targetCharacter:FindFirstChild("ReviveAttachment", true)
				local prompt = attachment and attachment:FindFirstChild("RevivePrompt", true)
				if prompt and prompt:IsA("ProximityPrompt") and prompt.Enabled and targetRoot
					and (root.Position - targetRoot.Position).Magnitude <= 50
					and (not reviveState.Triggered[prompt] or now - reviveState.Triggered[prompt] >= 0.1) then
					reviveState.Triggered[prompt] = now
					if type(fireproximityprompt) == "function" then
						local originalHoldDuration = prompt.HoldDuration
						prompt.HoldDuration = 0
						pcall(function() fireproximityprompt(prompt) end)
						task.delay(0.1, function()
							if prompt and prompt.Parent then prompt.HoldDuration = originalHoldDuration end
						end)
					end
				end
			end
		end
	end)

	HubState.Connections.QuietOrDieAutoKill = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
		if not killState.Enabled or not IsQuietOrDieKiller() or os.clock() - killState.LastAttack < 0.1 then return end
		local character = Player.Character
		local humanoid = character and character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
		local root = character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
		local playersFolder = workspace:FindFirstChild("PlayersFolder")
		local attackRemote = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("PlayerTouchedOrClicked")
		if not humanoid or humanoid.Health <= 0 or not root or not playersFolder or not attackRemote or not attackRemote:IsA("RemoteEvent") then return end

		local targets = {}
		for _, targetPlayer in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
			if targetPlayer ~= Player and playersFolder:FindFirstChild(targetPlayer.Name) then
				local targetCharacter = targetPlayer.Character
				local targetHumanoid = targetCharacter and targetCharacter:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
				local targetRoot = targetCharacter and targetCharacter:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
				if targetHumanoid and targetHumanoid.Health > 0 and targetRoot then table.insert(targets, targetRoot) end
			end
		end
		if #targets == 0 then return end

		killState.TargetIndex = (killState.TargetIndex % #targets) + 1
		local targetRoot = targets[killState.TargetIndex]
		root.CFrame = targetRoot.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 0, 2)
		root.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.zero
		killState.LastAttack = os.clock()
		pcall(function() attackRemote:FireServer() end)
	end)

	local function MuteQuietOrDieSound(sound)
		if not farmState.MuteAudio or not sound or not sound:IsA("Sound") then return end
		if farmState.MutedSounds[sound] == nil then farmState.MutedSounds[sound] = sound.Volume end
		sound.Volume = 0
	end

	farmState.SetAudioMuted = function(enabled)
		for _, connection in ipairs(farmState.AudioConnections) do connection:Disconnect() end
		farmState.AudioConnections = {}
		if not enabled then
			for sound, originalVolume in pairs(farmState.MutedSounds) do
				if sound and sound.Parent then sound.Volume = originalVolume end
			end
			farmState.MutedSounds = {}
			return
		end

		local pendingSounds = {}
		local processing = false
		local function queueSound(sound)
			if sound and sound:IsA("Sound") then table.insert(pendingSounds, sound) end
			if processing then return end
			processing = true
			task.spawn(function()
				while #pendingSounds > 0 and farmState.MuteAudio do
					for _ = 1, 8 do
						local nextSound = table.remove(pendingSounds, 1)
						if not nextSound then break end
						MuteQuietOrDieSound(nextSound)
					end
					task.wait()
				end
				processing = false
			end)
		end
		local function watchRoot(rootObject, scanExisting)
			if not rootObject then return end
			if rootObject:IsA("Sound") then queueSound(rootObject) end
			if scanExisting then
				task.spawn(function()
					local stack = rootObject:GetChildren()
					local scanned = 0
					while #stack > 0 and farmState.MuteAudio do
						local object = table.remove(stack)
						if not farmState.MuteAudio then break end
						if object:IsA("Sound") then queueSound(object) end
						for _, child in ipairs(object:GetChildren()) do
							table.insert(stack, child)
						end
						scanned = scanned + 1
						if scanned % 60 == 0 then task.wait() end
					end
				end)
			end
			table.insert(farmState.AudioConnections, rootObject.DescendantAdded:Connect(function(object)
				if object:IsA("Sound") then queueSound(object) end
			end))
		end

		local roots = {Player:FindFirstChild("Emote"), Player.Character, Player:FindFirstChildOfClass("PlayerGui"), workspace.CurrentCamera, game:GetService("SoundService"), workspace}
		for _, rootObject in ipairs(roots) do
			watchRoot(rootObject, true)
		end
		table.insert(farmState.AudioConnections, Player.ChildAdded:Connect(function(object)
			if object.Name == "Emote" then
				watchRoot(object, true)
			end
		end))
		table.insert(farmState.AudioConnections, Player.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(character)
			watchRoot(character, true)
		end))
	end

	farmState.SetUnclutter = function(enabled)
		farmState.SetAudioMuted(enabled)
	end
	ThemeObjects.RestoreQuietClutter = function() farmState.SetUnclutter(false) end

	local function TriggerQuietOrDieTaunt()
		local abilityEvent = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("AbilityEvent")
		if not abilityEvent or not abilityEvent:IsA("RemoteEvent") then return false end
		local fired = pcall(function() abilityEvent:FireServer(1) end)
		return fired
	end

	local resetCooldownEvent = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("ResetCooldownEvent")
	if resetCooldownEvent and resetCooldownEvent:IsA("RemoteEvent") then
		HubState.Connections.QuietOrDieResetCooldown = resetCooldownEvent.OnClientEvent:Connect(function()
			farmState.LastEmote = 0
		end)
	end

	HubState.Connections.QuietOrDieAutoFarm = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
		if not farmState.Enabled then return end
		if not IsQuietOrDieSurvivor() then return end
		local character = Player.Character
		local humanoid = character and character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
		local root = character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
		if not humanoid or humanoid.Health <= 0 or not root then return end
		if farmState.SafePlace and farmState.DroppedCharacter ~= character then
			farmState.DroppedCharacter = character
			ThemeObjects.SetRootUpright(root, root.CFrame, Vector3.new(-82, 53, -145))
			root.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.new(0, -3, 0)
		end
		local now = os.clock()
		if farmState.LastEmote ~= 0 and now - farmState.LastEmote < 0.18 then return end
		if TriggerQuietOrDieTaunt() then farmState.LastEmote = now end
	end)

	HubState.Connections.QuietOrDieAutoEvent = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
		if not eventState.Enabled then return end
		if IsQuietOrDieKiller() then eventState.Current = nil return end
		if os.clock() - eventState.LastMove < 0.06 then return end
		eventState.LastMove = os.clock()
		local character = Player.Character
		local humanoid = character and character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
		local root = character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
		local eventFolder = workspace:FindFirstChild("EventSpawns")
		if not humanoid or humanoid.Health <= 0 or not root or not eventFolder then return end

		local now = os.clock()
		for item, expiresAt in pairs(eventState.Skipped) do
			if not item.Parent or expiresAt <= now then eventState.Skipped[item] = nil end
		end

		local target = eventState.Current
		if not target or not target.Parent or eventState.Skipped[target] then
			target = nil
			local closestDistance = math.huge
			for _, item in ipairs(eventFolder:GetChildren()) do
				if item.Name:match("^EventItem%d+$") and not eventState.Skipped[item] then
					local part = item:IsA("BasePart") and item or item:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart", true)
					if part then
						local distance = (root.Position - part.Position).Magnitude
						if distance < closestDistance then
							closestDistance = distance
							target = item
						end
					end
				end
			end
			eventState.Current = target
			eventState.Started = now
		elseif now - eventState.Started > 1.5 then
			eventState.Skipped[target] = now + 2
			eventState.Current = nil
			return
		end

		if target and target.Parent then
			local targetPart = target:IsA("BasePart") and target or target:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart", true)
			if targetPart then
				ThemeObjects.SetRootUpright(root, root.CFrame, targetPart.Position + Vector3.new(0, -3.5, 0))
			end
		end
	end)

	gameButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		PlayClick()
		HubState.SelectedGame = "Quiet Or Die"
		HubState.PageHeader.Text = HubState.SelectedGame
		if HubState.GamesTabButton then HubState.GamesTabButton.Text = HubState.SelectedGame end
		HubState.MM2BackButton.Visible = true
		HubState.GamesPage.Visible = false
		HubState.GamesPage.Position = UDim2.new(1.1, 0, 0, 54)
		HubState.MM2Page.Visible = false
		HubState.MM2Page.Position = UDim2.new(1.1, 0, 0, 54)
		quietPage.Visible = true
		quietPage.Position = UDim2.new(0, 114, 0, 54)
		coinsDisplay.Visible = true
		winsDisplay.Visible = true
		historyButton.Visible = true
		ThemeObjects.ActiveTabName = "Games"
		HubState.ActiveTabIndex = table.find(HubState.TabNames, "Games") or HubState.ActiveTabIndex
		HubState.ActiveContentPage = quietPage
		UpdateTheme(true)
	end)
end

	if enabled and ThemeObjects.DisableOtherESP then ThemeObjects.DisableOtherESP("QOD") end
	ThemeObjects.DeepESP.Enabled = enabled == true
	ThemeObjects.DeepESP.Toggle.Text = ThemeObjects.DeepESP.Enabled and "On" or "Off"
	ThemeObjects.DeepESP.Title.TextColor3 = ThemeObjects.DeepESP.Enabled and AccentColor or InactiveTextColor()
	if not ThemeObjects.DeepESP.Enabled and ThemeObjects.ClearESPAdornments then ThemeObjects.ClearESPAdornments() end
	if not ThemeObjects.DeepESP.Enabled and not HubState.ESPEnabled and ThemeObjects.ClearESPLabels then ThemeObjects.ClearESPLabels() end
end

local function ToggleAutoLock()
	HubState.AutoLockEnabled = not HubState.AutoLockEnabled
	HubState.AutoLockToggleBtn.Text = HubState.AutoLockEnabled and "On" or "Off"
	HubState.AutoLockTitle.TextColor3 = HubState.AutoLockEnabled and AccentColor or InactiveTextColor()
end

ThemeObjects.ResolveESPCharacter = function(targetPlayer)
	if not targetPlayer then return nil end
	local character = targetPlayer.Character
	local playersFolder = workspace:FindFirstChild("PlayersFolder")
	local folderCharacter = playersFolder and playersFolder:FindFirstChild(targetPlayer.Name)
	local function hasCoreParts(model)
		if not model or not model:IsA("Model") then return false end
		return model:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid") ~= nil
			and (model:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or model:FindFirstChild("UpperTorso") or model:FindFirstChild("Torso") or model.PrimaryPart) ~= nil
	end
	if ThemeObjects.DeepESP and ThemeObjects.DeepESP.Enabled and hasCoreParts(folderCharacter) then return folderCharacter end
	if hasCoreParts(character) then return character end
	if hasCoreParts(folderCharacter) then return folderCharacter end
	return nil
end

ThemeObjects.IsBodyESPPart = function(part, character)
	if not part or not part:IsA("BasePart") or not character then return false end
	if part.Parent ~= character then return false end
	if part.Name == "HumanoidRootPart" then return true end
	return part.Name == "Head"
		or part.Name == "Torso"
		or part.Name == "UpperTorso"
		or part.Name == "LowerTorso"
		or part.Name == "LeftUpperArm"
		or part.Name == "LeftLowerArm"
		or part.Name == "LeftHand"
		or part.Name == "RightUpperArm"
		or part.Name == "RightLowerArm"
		or part.Name == "RightHand"
		or part.Name == "LeftUpperLeg"
		or part.Name == "LeftLowerLeg"
		or part.Name == "LeftFoot"
		or part.Name == "RightUpperLeg"
		or part.Name == "RightLowerLeg"
		or part.Name == "RightFoot"
		or part.Name == "Left Arm"
		or part.Name == "Right Arm"
		or part.Name == "Left Leg"
		or part.Name == "Right Leg"
end

ThemeObjects.ESPAdornmentRoot = Instance.new("Folder")
ThemeObjects.ESPAdornmentRoot.Name = "HqydeuESPAdornments"
ThemeObjects.ESPAdornmentRoot.Parent = ScreenGui
ThemeObjects.ESPAdornments = {}
ThemeObjects.ESPHighlights = {}
ThemeObjects.ClearESPAdornments = function(targetPlayer)
	if targetPlayer then
		if ThemeObjects.ESPHighlights[targetPlayer] then
			ThemeObjects.ESPHighlights[targetPlayer]:Destroy()
			ThemeObjects.ESPHighlights[targetPlayer] = nil
		end
		local adornments = ThemeObjects.ESPAdornments[targetPlayer]
		if adornments then
			for _, adornment in pairs(adornments) do
				if adornment then adornment:Destroy() end
			end
			ThemeObjects.ESPAdornments[targetPlayer] = nil
		end
		return
	end
	for playerObject, highlight in pairs(ThemeObjects.ESPHighlights) do
		if highlight then highlight:Destroy() end
		ThemeObjects.ESPHighlights[playerObject] = nil
	end
	for playerObject, adornments in pairs(ThemeObjects.ESPAdornments) do
		for _, adornment in pairs(adornments) do
			if adornment then adornment:Destroy() end
		end
		ThemeObjects.ESPAdornments[playerObject] = nil
	end
end
ThemeObjects.ClearESPLabels = function(targetPlayer)
	local function clearForPlayer(playerObject)
		local character = ThemeObjects.ResolveESPCharacter(playerObject)
		if not character then return end
		local head = character:FindFirstChild("Head")
		local root = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or character:FindFirstChild("UpperTorso") or character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or character.PrimaryPart
		if head and head:FindFirstChild("ESPGui") then head.ESPGui:Destroy() end
		if root and root:FindFirstChild("ESPGui") then root.ESPGui:Destroy() end
	end
	if targetPlayer then clearForPlayer(targetPlayer) return end
	for _, playerObject in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
		if playerObject ~= Player then clearForPlayer(playerObject) end
	end
end

ThemeObjects.DisableOtherESP = function(activeMode)
	return activeMode
end

local function ToggleESP()
	local nextEnabled = not HubState.ESPEnabled
	if nextEnabled and ThemeObjects.DisableOtherESP then ThemeObjects.DisableOtherESP("Player") end
	HubState.ESPEnabled = nextEnabled
	HubState.ESPToggleBtn.Text = HubState.ESPEnabled and "On" or "Off"
	HubState.ESPTitle.TextColor3 = HubState.ESPEnabled and AccentColor or InactiveTextColor()
	if not HubState.ESPEnabled then
		ThemeObjects.ClearESPAdornments()
		ThemeObjects.ClearESPLabels()
	end
end
ThemeObjects.DisableRegularESP = function()
	if HubState.ESPEnabled then ToggleESP() end
end
HubState.ESPToggleBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() PlayClick() ToggleESP() end)
HubState.Connections.ESPPlayerRemoving = Players.PlayerRemoving:Connect(function(leavingPlayer)
	ThemeObjects.ClearESPAdornments(leavingPlayer)
end)

local function RestoreAntiFlingCollisions()
	for part, originalCanCollide in pairs(HubState.AntiFlingOriginalCollision) do
		if part and part.Parent then part.CanCollide = originalCanCollide end
	end
	HubState.AntiFlingOriginalCollision = {}
end

local function FlingPlayer(targetPlayer)
	if HubState.Flinging or not targetPlayer or targetPlayer == Player then return end
	local character = Player.Character
	local humanoid = character and character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
	local root = character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
	local targetCharacter = targetPlayer.Character
	local targetHumanoid = targetCharacter and targetCharacter:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
	local targetRoot = targetCharacter and targetCharacter:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
	if not humanoid or humanoid.Health <= 0 or not root or not targetHumanoid or targetHumanoid.Health <= 0 or not targetRoot then return end

	HubState.Flinging = true
	local originalCFrame = root.CFrame
	local originalAutoRotate = humanoid.AutoRotate
	local originalPlatformStand = humanoid.PlatformStand
	local originalRootCollision = root.CanCollide
	local originalAngularVelocity = root.AssemblyAngularVelocity
	local originalLinearVelocity = root.AssemblyLinearVelocity
	local originalPartStates = {}
	local movers = {}
	humanoid.AutoRotate = false
	humanoid.PlatformStand = true
	pcall(function() humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Physics) end)
	root.CanCollide = true
	for _, part in ipairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
		if part:IsA("BasePart") then
			originalPartStates[part] = {
				CanCollide = part.CanCollide,
				Massless = part.Massless,
				CustomPhysicalProperties = part.CustomPhysicalProperties,
			}
			part.CanCollide = true
			part.Massless = false
			part.CustomPhysicalProperties = PhysicalProperties.new(100, 0.3, 0.5)
		end
	end

	local angularVelocity = Instance.new("BodyAngularVelocity")
	angularVelocity.Name = "R15FlingVelocity"
	angularVelocity.AngularVelocity = Vector3.new(0, 9000000, 0)
	angularVelocity.MaxTorque = Vector3.new(math.huge, math.huge, math.huge)
	angularVelocity.P = math.huge
	angularVelocity.Parent = root
	table.insert(movers, angularVelocity)

	local bodyVelocity = Instance.new("BodyVelocity")
	bodyVelocity.Name = "R15FlingPush"
	bodyVelocity.MaxForce = Vector3.new(math.huge, math.huge, math.huge)
	bodyVelocity.P = 125000
	bodyVelocity.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
	bodyVelocity.Parent = root
	table.insert(movers, bodyVelocity)

	local function cleanup()
		for _, mover in ipairs(movers) do
			if mover and mover.Parent then mover:Destroy() end
		end
		for part, state in pairs(originalPartStates) do
			if part and part.Parent then
				part.CanCollide = state.CanCollide
				part.Massless = state.Massless
				part.CustomPhysicalProperties = state.CustomPhysicalProperties
			end
		end
		if root and root.Parent then
			root.CanCollide = originalRootCollision
			root.AssemblyAngularVelocity = originalAngularVelocity
			root.AssemblyLinearVelocity = originalLinearVelocity
			root.CFrame = originalCFrame
		end
		if humanoid and humanoid.Parent then
			humanoid.AutoRotate = originalAutoRotate
			humanoid.PlatformStand = originalPlatformStand
			pcall(function() humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.GettingUp) end)
		end
		HubState.Flinging = false
	end

	pcall(function()
		local targetContactPart = targetCharacter:FindFirstChild("UpperTorso")
			or targetCharacter:FindFirstChild("Torso")
			or targetCharacter:FindFirstChild("LowerTorso")
			or targetRoot
		local yOffsets = {0, 1.15, -0.85, 0.45, -0.35}
		local radiusSteps = {0.1, 0.65, 1.25, 0.35, 0.95}
		local startedAt = os.clock()
		local step = 0
		local lastHardPass = 0
		while os.clock() - startedAt < 3.65 and targetRoot.Parent and targetHumanoid.Health > 0 and root.Parent and humanoid.Health > 0 do
			step += 1
			targetContactPart = targetCharacter:FindFirstChild("UpperTorso")
				or targetCharacter:FindFirstChild("Torso")
				or targetCharacter:FindFirstChild("LowerTorso")
				or targetRoot
			local targetPosition = targetContactPart.Position + (targetRoot.AssemblyLinearVelocity * 0.13)
			local angle = step * 1.75
			local radius = radiusSteps[((step - 1) % #radiusSteps) + 1]
			local yOffset = yOffsets[((step - 1) % #yOffsets) + 1]
			local orbitOffset = Vector3.new(math.cos(angle) * radius, yOffset, math.sin(angle) * radius)
			local passPosition = targetPosition + orbitOffset
			root.CFrame = CFrame.lookAt(passPosition, targetPosition) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(90), 0, 0)
			local pushDirection = (targetPosition - root.Position)
			if pushDirection.Magnitude < 0.05 then pushDirection = Vector3.new(0, 1, 0) end
			local verticalBoost = Vector3.new(0, (step % 2 == 0) and 220 or -90, 0)
			local pushVelocity = pushDirection.Unit * 620 + targetRoot.AssemblyLinearVelocity + verticalBoost
			if os.clock() - lastHardPass >= 0.12 then
				lastHardPass = os.clock()
				pushVelocity = pushVelocity + Vector3.new(0, 420, 0)
			end
			root.AssemblyAngularVelocity = Vector3.new(0, 9000000, 0)
			root.AssemblyLinearVelocity = pushVelocity
			bodyVelocity.Velocity = pushVelocity
			if os.clock() - startedAt > 0.85 and targetRoot.AssemblyLinearVelocity.Magnitude > 180 then break end
			RunService.Heartbeat:Wait()
		end
	end)
	cleanup()
end

local function RefreshFlingTargets()
	for _, child in ipairs(HubState.TargetScroll:GetChildren()) do
		if child:IsA("Frame") then child:Destroy() end
	end

	local filter = HubState.TargetSearch.Text:lower()
	for _, targetPlayer in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
		if targetPlayer ~= Player then
			local displayText = targetPlayer.DisplayName or targetPlayer.Name
			if filter == "" or displayText:lower():find(filter, 1, true) or targetPlayer.Name:lower():find(filter, 1, true) then
				local targetRow = Instance.new("Frame")
				targetRow.Name = "TargetRow"
				targetRow.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 30)
				targetRow.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(55, 55, 55)
				targetRow.BackgroundTransparency = 0.8
				targetRow.BorderSizePixel = 0
				targetRow.Parent = HubState.TargetScroll
				Instance.new("UICorner", targetRow).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4)
				ThemeObjects.StyleControlOutline(targetRow)

				local displayLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
				displayLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, -12, 0, 16)
				displayLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 7, 0, 1)
				displayLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
				displayLabel.Text = displayText
				displayLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
				displayLabel.TextSize = 10
				displayLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
				displayLabel.Parent = targetRow
				table.insert(ThemeObjects.Texts, displayLabel)

				local usernameLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
				usernameLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, -12, 0, 11)
				usernameLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 7, 0, 16)
				usernameLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
				usernameLabel.Text = "@" .. targetPlayer.Name
				usernameLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
				usernameLabel.TextSize = 8
				usernameLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
				usernameLabel.TextTransparency = 0
				usernameLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
				usernameLabel.Parent = targetRow
				table.insert(ThemeObjects.Texts, usernameLabel)

				local targetButton = Instance.new("TextButton")
				targetButton.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
				targetButton.BackgroundTransparency = 1
				targetButton.Text = ""
				targetButton.Parent = targetRow
				targetButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
					PlayClick()
					task.spawn(FlingPlayer, targetPlayer)
				end)
			end
		end
	end
	HubState.TargetScroll.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, HubState.TargetListLayout.AbsoluteContentSize.Y + 2)
	UpdateTheme()
end

HubState.TargetSearch:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Text"):Connect(RefreshFlingTargets)
TrackConnection("FlingTargetsPlayerAdded", Players.PlayerAdded:Connect(RefreshFlingTargets))
TrackConnection("FlingTargetsPlayerRemoving", Players.PlayerRemoving:Connect(RefreshFlingTargets))

local function ToggleFlingMenu()
	PlaySwoosh()
	if not HubState.TargetFrame.Visible then RefreshFlingTargets() end
	HubState.TargetFrame.Visible = not HubState.TargetFrame.Visible
end
ThemeObjects.AddFeatureKeybind({Name = "Fling Menu", Storage = "FlingMenu", Button = HubState.FlingBindBtn, Get = function() return HubState.FlingMenuKeybind end, Set = function(key) HubState.FlingMenuKeybind = key; SaveKeybind("FlingMenu", key); if HubState.FlingBindBtn then HubState.FlingBindBtn.Text = KeybindText(key) end end, Action = ToggleFlingMenu})

HubState.FlingTargetBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() PlayClick() ToggleFlingMenu() end)
