ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.Refresh = function()
	for _, child in ipairs(ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.Scroll:GetChildren()) do
		if child:IsA("Frame") then child:Destroy() end
	end
	local filter = ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.Search.Text:lower()
	for _, targetPlayer in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
		if targetPlayer ~= Player then
			local displayText = targetPlayer.DisplayName or targetPlayer.Name
			if filter == "" or displayText:lower():find(filter, 1, true) or targetPlayer.Name:lower():find(filter, 1, true) then
				local targetRow = Instance.new("Frame")
				targetRow.Name = "PlayerTPRow"
				targetRow.Size = UDim2.new(1, -8, 0, 30)
				targetRow.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(55, 55, 55)
				targetRow.BackgroundTransparency = 1
				targetRow.BorderSizePixel = 0
				targetRow.Parent = ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.Scroll
				Instance.new("UICorner", targetRow).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4)

				local displayLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
				displayLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, -12, 0, 16)
				displayLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 7, 0, 1)
				displayLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
				displayLabel.Text = displayText
				displayLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
				displayLabel.TextSize = 10
				displayLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
				displayLabel.TextTransparency = 0
				displayLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
				displayLabel.Parent = targetRow

			local usernameLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
				usernameLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, -12, 0, 11)
				usernameLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 7, 0, 16)
				usernameLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
				usernameLabel.Text = "@" .. targetPlayer.Name
				usernameLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
				usernameLabel.TextSize = 8
				usernameLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
				usernameLabel.TextTransparency = 0
				usernameLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
				usernameLabel.Parent = targetRow

				local targetButton = Instance.new("TextButton")
				targetButton.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
				targetButton.BackgroundTransparency = 1
				targetButton.Text = ""
				targetButton.Parent = targetRow
				targetButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
					PlayClick()
					local targetCharacter = targetPlayer.Character
					local targetRoot = targetCharacter and targetCharacter:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
					local character = Player.Character
					local root = character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
					if targetRoot and root then root.CFrame = targetRoot.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 0, 3) end
				end)
			end
		end
	end
	ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.Scroll.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.Layout.AbsoluteContentSize.Y + 2)
end

ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.ShowTab = function(tabName)
	ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.ActiveTab = tabName == "Waypoints" and "Waypoints" or "Players"
	local showingWaypoints = ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.ActiveTab == "Waypoints"
	ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.Search.Visible = not showingWaypoints
	ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.Scroll.Visible = not showingWaypoints
	ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.WaypointSearch.Visible = showingWaypoints
	ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.WaypointScroll.Visible = showingWaypoints
	ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.PlayersTab.BackgroundTransparency = showingWaypoints and 0.55 or 0.18
	ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.WaypointsTab.BackgroundTransparency = showingWaypoints and 0.18 or 0.55
	ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.PlayersTab.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
	ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.WaypointsTab.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
	if showingWaypoints and ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.RefreshWaypoints then ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.RefreshWaypoints()
	else ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.Refresh() end
end

ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.Toggle = function()
	PlaySwoosh()
	if not ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.Frame.Visible then ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.ShowTab(ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.ActiveTab or "Players") end
	ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.Frame.Visible = not ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.Frame.Visible
end

	if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
		ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.Dragging = true
		ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.DragStart = input.Position
		ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.StartPosition = ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.Frame.Position
		input.Changed:Connect(function()
			if input.UserInputState == Enum.UserInputState.End then ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.Dragging = false end
		end)
	end
end)
TrackConnection("PlayerTPDragMove", UserInputService.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
	if ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.Dragging and (input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch) then
		local delta = input.Position - ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.DragStart
		ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.Frame.Position = UDim2.new(ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.StartPosition.X.Scale, ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.StartPosition.X.Offset + delta.X, ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.StartPosition.Y.Scale, ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.StartPosition.Y.Offset + delta.Y)
	end
end))


HubState.FlingBindBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
	PlayClick()
	if HubState.FlingBindConnection then
		HubState.FlingBindConnection:Disconnect()
		HubState.FlingBindConnection = nil
	end
	HubState.IsBindingFlingMenu = true
	HubState.FlingBindBtn.Text = "..."
	HubState.FlingBindConnection = UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, processed)
		if processed then return end
		if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Keyboard then
			local selectedKey = input.KeyCode
			if selectedKey == Enum.KeyCode.Backspace or selectedKey == Enum.KeyCode.Delete then
				selectedKey = Enum.KeyCode.Unknown
			end
			HubState.FlingMenuKeybind = selectedKey
			SaveKeybind("FlingMenu", selectedKey)
			HubState.FlingBindBtn.Text = KeybindText(selectedKey)
			HubState.IsBindingFlingMenu = false
			if HubState.FlingBindConnection then
				HubState.FlingBindConnection:Disconnect()
				HubState.FlingBindConnection = nil
			end
		end
	end)
end)

end})

function ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.GetSegments(instance)
	local segments = {}
	local current = instance
	while current and current ~= game do
		table.insert(segments, 1, current.Name)
		current = current.Parent
	end
	return segments
end

function ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.Resolve(waypoint)
	local segments = waypoint.Segments
	if type(segments) ~= "table" or #segments == 0 then return nil end
	local current = game
	for _, name in ipairs(segments) do
		if current == game then
			local success, service = pcall(function() return game:GetService(name) end)
			current = success and service or game:FindFirstChild(name)
		else
			current = current and current:FindFirstChild(name)
		end
		if not current then return nil end
	end
	if current:IsA("BasePart") then return current end
	return nil
end

function ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.GetCFrame(waypoint)
	if type(waypoint.CFrame) == "table" and #waypoint.CFrame >= 12 then
		return CFrame.new(table.unpack(waypoint.CFrame, 1, 12))
	end
	local part = ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.Resolve(waypoint)
	return part and part.CFrame or nil
end

function ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.Save()
	local serializable = {}
	for _, waypoint in ipairs(ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.Waypoints) do
		table.insert(serializable, {Segments = waypoint.Segments, CFrame = waypoint.CFrame, Name = waypoint.Name, Kind = waypoint.Kind})
	end
	SavedKeybinds.WaypointsByPlace[ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.StorageKey] = serializable
	SavePersistentSettings()
end

function ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.Refresh()
	for _, child in ipairs(ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.List:GetChildren()) do
		if child:IsA("Frame") then child:Destroy() end
	end
	for index, waypoint in ipairs(ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.Waypoints) do
		local waypointRow = Instance.new("Frame")
		waypointRow.Name = "Waypoint" .. index
		waypointRow.Size = UDim2.new(1, -10, 0, 34)
		waypointRow.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(38, 38, 52)
		waypointRow.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		waypointRow.Parent = ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.List
		Instance.new("UICorner", waypointRow).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4)

		local waypointButton = Instance.new("TextButton")
		waypointButton.Size = UDim2.new(1, -72, 1, -8)
		waypointButton.Position = UDim2.new(0, 8, 0, 4)
		waypointButton.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		waypointButton.BorderSizePixel = 0
		waypointButton.Text = waypoint.Name or "Waypoint"
		waypointButton.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
		waypointButton.TextSize = 10
		waypointButton.TextTruncate = Enum.TextTruncate.AtEnd
		waypointButton.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
		waypointButton.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
		waypointButton.Parent = waypointRow
		table.insert(ThemeObjects.Texts, waypointButton)
		Instance.new("UICorner", waypointButton).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4)

		local editButton = Instance.new("TextButton")
		editButton.Size = UDim2.new(0, 36, 1, -8)
		editButton.Position = UDim2.new(1, -62, 0, 4)
		editButton.BackgroundColor3 = AccentColor
		editButton.BorderSizePixel = 0
		editButton.Text = "Edit"
		editButton.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
		editButton.TextSize = 8
		editButton.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
		editButton.Parent = waypointRow
		table.insert(ThemeObjects.AccentBackgrounds, editButton)
		Instance.new("UICorner", editButton).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4)

		local deleteButton = Instance.new("TextButton")
		deleteButton.Size = UDim2.new(0, 22, 1, -8)
		deleteButton.Position = UDim2.new(1, -24, 0, 4)
		deleteButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 35, 35)
		deleteButton.BackgroundTransparency = 0
		deleteButton.BorderSizePixel = 0
		deleteButton.Text = "×"
		deleteButton.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
		deleteButton.TextSize = 11
		deleteButton.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
		deleteButton.Parent = waypointRow
		Instance.new("UICorner", deleteButton).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4)

		waypointButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			PlayClick()
			local waypointCFrame = ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.GetCFrame(waypoint)
			local character = Player.Character
			local root = character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
			if waypointCFrame and root then
				root.CFrame = waypoint.Kind == "Position" and waypointCFrame or waypointCFrame * CFrame.new(0, 3, 0)
			end
		end)
		editButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			PlayClick()
			waypointButton.Visible = false
			editButton.Visible = false
			local editBox = Instance.new("TextBox")
			editBox.Size = UDim2.new(1, -25, 1, 0)
			editBox.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(45, 45, 45)
			editBox.BackgroundTransparency = 0.8
			editBox.BorderSizePixel = 0
			editBox.Text = waypoint.Name or "Waypoint"
			editBox.PlaceholderText = "Waypoint name..."
			editBox.PlaceholderColor3 = InactiveTextColor()
			editBox.ClearTextOnFocus = false
			editBox.Font = waypointButton.Font
			editBox.TextSize = waypointButton.TextSize
			editBox.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Center
			editBox.TextWrapped = false
			editBox.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
			editBox.Parent = waypointRow
			table.insert(ThemeObjects.Texts, editBox)
			Instance.new("UICorner", editBox).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4)
			editBox.FocusLost:Connect(function()
				local newName = editBox.Text:match("^%s*(.-)%s*$")
				if newName and newName ~= "" then waypoint.Name = string.sub(newName, 1, 32) end
				ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.Save()
				ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.Refresh()
			end)
			task.defer(function() editBox:CaptureFocus() end)
		end)
		deleteButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			PlayClick()
			table.remove(ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.Waypoints, index)
			ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.Save()
			ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.Refresh()
		end)
	end
	ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.List.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.Layout.AbsoluteContentSize.Y + 8)
	if ThemeObjects.PlayerTP and ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.RefreshWaypoints then ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.RefreshWaypoints() end
	UpdateTheme(true)
end

ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.RefreshWaypoints = function()

		if child:IsA("Frame") then child:Destroy() end

ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.AddWaypoint = function(part)
	if not part or not part:IsA("BasePart") then return end
	local segments = ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.GetSegments(part)
	local components = {part.CFrame:GetComponents()}
	local signature = table.concat(components, ",")
	for _, waypoint in ipairs(ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.Waypoints) do
		if table.concat(waypoint.CFrame or {}, ",") == signature then return end
	end
	table.insert(ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.Waypoints, {Segments = segments, CFrame = components, Name = part.Name})
	ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.Save()
	ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.Refresh()
end

ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.AddButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
	PlayClick()
	if ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Selecting then ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.EndSelection(true)
	else ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.BeginSelection("Waypoint") end
end)
ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.CurrentButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
	PlayClick()
	if ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.Selecting then ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.EndSelection(true) end
	local character = Player.Character
	local root = character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
	if not root then return end
	local components = {root.CFrame:GetComponents()}
	local signature = table.concat(components, ",")
	for _, waypoint in ipairs(ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.Waypoints) do
		if table.concat(waypoint.CFrame or {}, ",") == signature then return end
	end
	table.insert(ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.Waypoints, {
		Segments = {},
		CFrame = components,
		Name = "Current Position",
		Kind = "Position"
	})
	ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.Save()
	ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.Refresh()
end)
ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.Refresh()

ThemeObjects.ShowWaypointsPage = function(showWaypoints)
	ThemeObjects.WaypointsOpen = showWaypoints == true
	if ThemeObjects.WaypointsOpen then HubState.PlayerSearch.Visible = false end
	HubState.PlayerScroll.Visible = not ThemeObjects.WaypointsOpen
	ThemeObjects.WaypointUI.Frame.Visible = ThemeObjects.WaypointsOpen
	ThemeObjects.WaypointToggleButton.Text = ThemeObjects.WaypointsOpen and "Players" or "Waypoints"
end
ThemeObjects.WaypointToggleButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
	PlayClick()
	ThemeObjects.ShowWaypointsPage(not ThemeObjects.WaypointsOpen)
end)
ThemeObjects.ShowWaypointsPage(false)

local function UpdatePlayerList()
	ThemeObjects.PlayerListReady = true
	for _, item in pairs(HubState.PlayerScroll:GetChildren()) do
		if item:IsA("Frame") then item:Destroy() end
	end
	for _, p in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
		if p == Player then continue end
		local pFrame = Instance.new("Frame")
		pFrame.Name = p.Name
		pFrame.Size = UDim2.new(1, -4, 0, 34)
		pFrame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(38, 38, 52)
		pFrame.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		pFrame.BorderSizePixel = 0
		pFrame.Parent = HubState.PlayerScroll
		Instance.new("UICorner", pFrame).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4)

		local pName = Instance.new("TextLabel")
		pName.Size = UDim2.new(1, -46, 1, 0)
		pName.Position = UDim2.new(0, 8, 0, 0)
		pName.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		pName.BorderSizePixel = 0
		pName.Text = p.DisplayName or p.Name
		pName.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
		pName.TextSize = 11
		pName.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
		pName.TextTransparency = 0
		pName.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
		pName.Parent = pFrame
		table.insert(ThemeObjects.Texts, pName)

		local tpBtn = Instance.new("TextButton")
		tpBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0, 42, 0, 22)
		tpBtn.Position = UDim2.new(1, -50, 0.5, -11)
		tpBtn.BackgroundColor3 = AccentColor
		tpBtn.BackgroundTransparency = 0.3
		tpBtn.BorderSizePixel = 0
		tpBtn.Text = "TP"
		tpBtn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
		tpBtn.TextSize = 10
		tpBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
		tpBtn.Parent = pFrame
		table.insert(ThemeObjects.Backgrounds, tpBtn)
		table.insert(ThemeObjects.Accents, tpBtn)

		local tpCorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
		tpCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4)
		tpCorner.Parent = tpBtn

		local divider = Instance.new("Frame")
		divider.Name = "PlayerDivider"
		divider.Size = UDim2.new(1, -12, 0, 1)
		divider.Position = UDim2.new(0, 6, 1, -1)
		divider.BackgroundColor3 = AccentColor
		divider.BackgroundTransparency = 0.08
		divider.BorderSizePixel = 0
		divider.Parent = pFrame
		table.insert(ThemeObjects.AccentBackgrounds, divider)

		tpBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			PlayClick()
			if p.Character and p.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and Player.Character and Player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
				Player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = p.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 0, 3)
			end
		end)
	end
	HubState.PlayerScroll.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, HubState.PlayerListLayout.AbsoluteContentSize.Y)
end

HubState.PlayerSearch:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Text"):Connect(function()
	local filter = HubState.PlayerSearch.Text:lower()
	for _, frame in pairs(HubState.PlayerScroll:GetChildren()) do
		if frame:IsA("Frame") then
			frame.Visible = (frame.Name:lower():find(filter) or (frame:FindFirstChildOfClass("TextLabel") and frame:FindFirstChildOfClass("TextLabel").Text:lower():find(filter))) and true or false
		end
	end
	HubState.PlayerScroll.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, HubState.PlayerListLayout.AbsoluteContentSize.Y)
end)

TrackConnection("TeleportPlayerAdded", Players.PlayerAdded:Connect(UpdatePlayerList))
TrackConnection("TeleportPlayerRemoving", Players.PlayerRemoving:Connect(UpdatePlayerList))

HubState.CoinFarmStatus.Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium

HubState.CoinFarmStatus.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)

HubState.CoinFarmStatus.Parent = HubState.MM2Page

HubState.CoinFarmEnabled = false
HubState.CoinFarmConnection = nil
HubState.LastCoinRefresh = 0
HubState.CachedCoins = {}
HubState.CurrentCoin = nil
HubState.CurrentCoinStartedAt = 0
HubState.CoinCollectionTimeout = 1.25
HubState.SkippedCoins = {}
HubState.AutoGunPickupBusy = false

local function GetAllCoins()
	local now = os.clock()
	if now - HubState.LastCoinRefresh < 0.5 then
		return HubState.CachedCoins
	end
	HubState.LastCoinRefresh = now
	HubState.CachedCoins = {}
	for _, obj in ipairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
		if obj:IsA("BasePart") and obj.Name == "Coin_Server" and obj.Parent and obj.Parent.Name == "CoinContainer" then
			table.insert(HubState.CachedCoins, obj)
		end
	end
	return HubState.CachedCoins
end

local function EnableUndergroundMode(root)
	if not root then return end
	root.CanCollide = false
	for _, part in pairs(Player.Character:GetDescendants()) do
		if part:IsA("BasePart") then
			part.CanCollide = false
		end
	end
end

local function StartCoinFarm()
	if HubState.CoinFarmConnection then HubState.CoinFarmConnection:Disconnect() end
	HubState.CurrentCoin = nil
	HubState.CurrentCoinStartedAt = 0
	HubState.SkippedCoins = {}
	
	HubState.CoinFarmConnection = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
		if not HubState.CoinFarmEnabled then return end
		if HubState.AutoGunPickupBusy then return end
		
		local coins = GetAllCoins()
		if #coins == 0 then
			HubState.CoinFarmStatus.Text = "0"
			return
		end
		
		local root = Player.Character and Player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
		if not root then return end
		local now = os.clock()
		local availableCoins = {}
		for _, coin in ipairs(coins) do
			local skipUntil = HubState.SkippedCoins[coin]
			if not skipUntil or now >= skipUntil then
				HubState.SkippedCoins[coin] = nil
				table.insert(availableCoins, coin)
			end
		end

		if #availableCoins == 0 then
			HubState.CoinFarmStatus.Text = tostring(#coins)
			return
		end
		
		table.sort(availableCoins, function(a, b)
			return (root.Position - a.Position).Magnitude < (root.Position - b.Position).Magnitude
		end)
		
		local target = availableCoins[1]
		if target and target.Parent then
			if HubState.CurrentCoin ~= target then
				HubState.CurrentCoin = target
				HubState.CurrentCoinStartedAt = now
			elseif now - HubState.CurrentCoinStartedAt >= HubState.CoinCollectionTimeout then
				HubState.SkippedCoins[target] = now + 4
				HubState.CurrentCoin = nil
				HubState.CoinFarmStatus.Text = tostring(#coins)
				return
			end

			HubState.CoinFarmStatus.Text = tostring(#coins)
			ThemeObjects.SetRootUpright(root, root.CFrame, target.Position + Vector3.new(0, -3.5, 0))
			-- Extremely minimal delay for maximum speed
			task.wait(0.001)
		end
	end)
end

local function ToggleCoinFarm()
	HubState.CoinFarmEnabled = not HubState.CoinFarmEnabled
	HubState.CoinFarmToggle.Text = HubState.CoinFarmEnabled and "On" or "Off"
	HubState.CoinFarmTitle.TextColor3 = HubState.CoinFarmEnabled and AccentColor or InactiveTextColor()
	
	if HubState.CoinFarmEnabled then
		HubState.CoinFarmStatus.Text = "0"
		local root = Player.Character and Player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
		if root then EnableUndergroundMode(root) end
		StartCoinFarm()
	else
		HubState.CoinFarmStatus.Text = "0"
		if HubState.CoinFarmConnection then
			HubState.CoinFarmConnection:Disconnect()
			HubState.CoinFarmConnection = nil
		end
		local root = Player.Character and Player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
		if root and Player.Character then
			root.CanCollide = true
			for _, part in pairs(Player.Character:GetDescendants()) do
				if part:IsA("BasePart") then part.CanCollide = true end
			end
		end
	end
end

HubState.CoinFarmToggle.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
	PlayClick()
	ToggleCoinFarm()
end)

HubState.GunDropESP = {Enabled = false, Highlight = nil, Adornee = nil, LastCheck = 0}

HubState.AutoGunPickupEnabled = false
HubState.LastGunDrop = nil
HubState.GunPickupDelay = 0.5

local function FindGunDrop()
	for _, map in ipairs(workspace:GetChildren()) do
		local gunDrop = map:FindFirstChild("GunDrop")
		if gunDrop then return gunDrop end
	end
	return nil
end

function HubState.GunDropESP.Clear()
	if HubState.GunDropESP.Highlight then HubState.GunDropESP.Highlight:Destroy() end
	if HubState.GunDropESP.Label then HubState.GunDropESP.Label:Destroy() end
	HubState.GunDropESP.Highlight = nil
	HubState.GunDropESP.Label = nil
	HubState.GunDropESP.Adornee = nil
end

function HubState.GunDropESP.Refresh()
	if not HubState.GunDropESP.Enabled then
		HubState.GunDropESP.Clear()
		return
	end

	local gunDrop = FindGunDrop()
	if not gunDrop or not gunDrop.Parent then
		HubState.GunDropESP.Clear()
		return
	end
	if gunDrop == HubState.GunDropESP.Adornee and HubState.GunDropESP.Highlight and HubState.GunDropESP.Highlight.Parent then return end

	HubState.GunDropESP.Clear()
	HubState.GunDropESP.Adornee = gunDrop
	HubState.GunDropESP.Highlight = Instance.new("Highlight")
	HubState.GunDropESP.Highlight.Name = "HqydeuGunDropESP"
	HubState.GunDropESP.Highlight.Adornee = gunDrop
	HubState.GunDropESP.Highlight.FillColor = Color3.fromRGB(255, 205, 65)
	HubState.GunDropESP.Highlight.FillTransparency = 0.18
	HubState.GunDropESP.Highlight.OutlineColor = Color3.fromRGB(255, 245, 190)
	HubState.GunDropESP.Highlight.OutlineTransparency = 0
	HubState.GunDropESP.Highlight.DepthMode = Enum.HighlightDepthMode.AlwaysOnTop
	HubState.GunDropESP.Highlight.Parent = gunDrop

	local labelPart = gunDrop:IsA("BasePart") and gunDrop or gunDrop:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart", true)
	if labelPart then
		HubState.GunDropESP.Label = Instance.new("BillboardGui")
		HubState.GunDropESP.Label.Name = "HqydeuGunDropLabel"
		HubState.GunDropESP.Label.Adornee = labelPart
		HubState.GunDropESP.Label.Size = UDim2.new(0, 64, 0, 20)
		HubState.GunDropESP.Label.StudsOffsetWorldSpace = Vector3.new(0, 2.2, 0)
		HubState.GunDropESP.Label.AlwaysOnTop = true
		HubState.GunDropESP.Label.Parent = gunDrop
		local labelText = Instance.new("TextLabel")
		labelText.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
		labelText.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		labelText.Text = "Gun"
		labelText.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
		labelText.TextSize = 12
		labelText.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 225, 80)
		labelText.TextStrokeColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(25, 25, 25)
		labelText.TextStrokeTransparency = 0.2
		labelText.Parent = HubState.GunDropESP.Label
	end
end

HubState.Connections.GunDropESP = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
	if os.clock() - HubState.GunDropESP.LastCheck < 0.2 then return end
	HubState.GunDropESP.LastCheck = os.clock()
	HubState.GunDropESP.Refresh()
end)

local function GetGunDropCFrame(gunDrop)
	if gunDrop:IsA("BasePart") then
		return gunDrop.CFrame
	elseif gunDrop:IsA("Model") then
		local part = gunDrop.PrimaryPart or gunDrop:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart", true)
		return part and part.CFrame or nil
	end
	return nil
end

local function IsAliveAndInsideActiveMap(gunDrop)
	local character = Player.Character
	local humanoid = character and character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
	local root = character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
	if not humanoid or humanoid.Health <= 0 or not root then return false end

	local map = gunDrop and gunDrop.Parent
	if not map or map.Parent ~= workspace then return false end

	if map:IsA("Model") then
		local mapCFrame, mapSize = map:GetBoundingBox()
		local localPosition = mapCFrame:PointToObjectSpace(root.Position)
		local padding = Vector3.new(20, 20, 20)
		local halfSize = (mapSize / 2) + padding
		return math.abs(localPosition.X) <= halfSize.X
			and math.abs(localPosition.Y) <= halfSize.Y
			and math.abs(localPosition.Z) <= halfSize.Z
	end

	return false
end

local function TryPickUpGun(gunDrop)
	if HubState.AutoGunPickupBusy or not HubState.AutoGunPickupEnabled or not gunDrop or not gunDrop.Parent then return end
	if not IsAliveAndInsideActiveMap(gunDrop) then return end
	local root = Player.Character and Player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
	local gunCFrame = GetGunDropCFrame(gunDrop)
	if not root or not gunCFrame then return end

	HubState.AutoGunPickupBusy = true
	local originalCFrame = root.CFrame
	root.CFrame = gunCFrame
	task.wait(0.15)
	if root and root.Parent then
		root.CFrame = originalCFrame
	end
	HubState.AutoGunPickupBusy = false
end

HubState.Connections.AutoGunPickup = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
	if not HubState.AutoGunPickupEnabled or HubState.AutoGunPickupBusy then return end
	local gunDrop = FindGunDrop()
	if not gunDrop then
		HubState.LastGunDrop = nil
		return
	end

	if gunDrop ~= HubState.LastGunDrop then
		HubState.LastGunDrop = gunDrop
		task.delay(HubState.GunPickupDelay, function()
			if HubState.LastGunDrop == gunDrop then
				TryPickUpGun(gunDrop)
			end
		end)
	end
end)

	PlayClick()
	HubState.AutoGunPickupEnabled = not HubState.AutoGunPickupEnabled
	HubState.AutoGunToggle.Text = HubState.AutoGunPickupEnabled and "On" or "Off"
	HubState.AutoGunTitle.TextColor3 = HubState.AutoGunPickupEnabled and AccentColor or InactiveTextColor()
	if HubState.AutoGunPickupEnabled then
		HubState.LastGunDrop = nil
	else
		HubState.LastGunDrop = nil
	end
end)

local function UpdateRoleHighlights()
	for _, targetPlayer in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
		local character = targetPlayer.Character
		if character then
			local isMurdererOverride = targetPlayer ~= Player and HubState.MurdererRoleESPEnabled and targetPlayer == HubState.CurrentMurderer
			local isSheriffOverride = targetPlayer ~= Player and HubState.SheriffRoleESPEnabled and targetPlayer == HubState.CurrentSheriff
			local roleOverride = isMurdererOverride or isSheriffOverride

			local murdererHighlight = character:FindFirstChild("MurdererRoleHighlight")
			local sheriffHighlight = character:FindFirstChild("SheriffRoleHighlight")
			if isMurdererOverride then
				if sheriffHighlight then sheriffHighlight:Destroy() end
				if not murdererHighlight then
					murdererHighlight = Instance.new("Highlight")
					murdererHighlight.Name = "MurdererRoleHighlight"
					murdererHighlight.Parent = character
				end
				murdererHighlight.FillColor = Color3.fromRGB(255, 70, 70)
				murdererHighlight.OutlineColor = Color3.fromRGB(255, 40, 40)
				murdererHighlight.FillTransparency = 0.72
				murdererHighlight.OutlineTransparency = 0
			else
				if murdererHighlight then murdererHighlight:Destroy() end
			end

			if isSheriffOverride then
				if not sheriffHighlight then
					sheriffHighlight = Instance.new("Highlight")
					sheriffHighlight.Name = "SheriffRoleHighlight"
					sheriffHighlight.Parent = character
				end
				sheriffHighlight.FillColor = Color3.fromRGB(70, 130, 255)
				sheriffHighlight.OutlineColor = Color3.fromRGB(40, 100, 255)
				sheriffHighlight.FillTransparency = 0.72
				sheriffHighlight.OutlineTransparency = 0
			else
				if sheriffHighlight then sheriffHighlight:Destroy() end
			end

			local regularHighlight = character:FindFirstChild("ESPHighlight")
			if regularHighlight then
				if roleOverride then regularHighlight:Destroy()
				else regularHighlight.Enabled = HubState.ESPEnabled end
			end
		end
	end
end

HubState.MurdererESPBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
	PlayClick()
	HubState.MurdererRoleESPEnabled = not HubState.MurdererRoleESPEnabled
	HubState.MurdererESPBtn.Text = HubState.MurdererRoleESPEnabled and "ON" or "ESP"
	if ThemeObjects.RefreshMM2RolesFromTools then ThemeObjects.RefreshMM2RolesFromTools() end
	if HubState.MurdererRoleESPEnabled and ThemeObjects.RefreshMM2RolesFromRemote then ThemeObjects.RefreshMM2RolesFromRemote() end
	UpdateRoleHighlights()
end)

HubState.SheriffESPBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
	PlayClick()
	HubState.SheriffRoleESPEnabled = not HubState.SheriffRoleESPEnabled
	HubState.SheriffESPBtn.Text = HubState.SheriffRoleESPEnabled and "ON" or "ESP"
	HubState.GunDropESP.Enabled = HubState.SheriffRoleESPEnabled
	HubState.GunDropESP.Refresh()
	if ThemeObjects.RefreshMM2RolesFromTools then ThemeObjects.RefreshMM2RolesFromTools() end
	if HubState.SheriffRoleESPEnabled and ThemeObjects.RefreshMM2RolesFromRemote then ThemeObjects.RefreshMM2RolesFromRemote() end
	UpdateRoleHighlights()
end)

ThemeObjects.SetMM2ESP = function(enabled)
	if enabled and ThemeObjects.DisableOtherESP then ThemeObjects.DisableOtherESP("MM2") end
	HubState.MM2ESPEnabled = enabled == true
	HubState.MurdererRoleESPEnabled = HubState.MM2ESPEnabled
	HubState.SheriffRoleESPEnabled = HubState.MM2ESPEnabled
	HubState.MurdererESPBtn.Text = HubState.MM2ESPEnabled and "ON" or "ESP"
	HubState.SheriffESPBtn.Text = HubState.MM2ESPEnabled and "ON" or "ESP"
	if HubState.MM2ESPToggle then HubState.MM2ESPToggle.Text = HubState.MM2ESPEnabled and "On" or "Off" end
	if HubState.MM2ESPTitle then HubState.MM2ESPTitle.TextColor3 = HubState.MM2ESPEnabled and AccentColor or InactiveTextColor() end
	HubState.GunDropESP.Enabled = HubState.MM2ESPEnabled
	HubState.GunDropESP.Refresh()
	if ThemeObjects.RefreshMM2RolesFromTools then ThemeObjects.RefreshMM2RolesFromTools() end
	if HubState.MM2ESPEnabled and ThemeObjects.RefreshMM2RolesFromRemote then ThemeObjects.RefreshMM2RolesFromRemote() end
	UpdateRoleHighlights()
end

local function PlayerHasRoleTool(targetPlayer, toolName)
	local wantedName = toolName:lower()
	local function ContainerHasTool(container)
		if container then
			for _, item in ipairs(container:GetChildren()) do
				if item.Name:lower() == wantedName then return true end
			end
		end
		return false
	end
	return ContainerHasTool(targetPlayer.Character) or ContainerHasTool(targetPlayer:FindFirstChild("Backpack"))
end

local function FormatRolePlayer(targetPlayer)
	if not targetPlayer then return "Unknown" end
	return string.format("%s (@%s)", targetPlayer.DisplayName or targetPlayer.Name, targetPlayer.Name)
end

HubState.LastMurdererAvatarId = 0
HubState.LastSheriffAvatarId = 0

local function UpdateRoleAvatar(imageLabel, targetPlayer, roleName)
	imageLabel.Image = ""
	if not targetPlayer then return end
	local expectedUserId = targetPlayer.UserId
	task.spawn(function()
		local success, image = pcall(function()
			return Players:GetUserThumbnailAsync(expectedUserId, Enum.ThumbnailType.HeadShot, Enum.ThumbnailSize.Size100x100)
		end)
		local stillCurrent = (roleName == "Murderer" and HubState.CurrentMurderer == targetPlayer)
			or (roleName == "Sheriff" and HubState.CurrentSheriff == targetPlayer)
		if success and stillCurrent then imageLabel.Image = image end
	end)
end

ThemeObjects.RefreshMM2RoleDisplay = function()
	local murdererAvatarId = HubState.CurrentMurderer and HubState.CurrentMurderer.UserId or 0
	local sheriffAvatarId = HubState.CurrentSheriff and HubState.CurrentSheriff.UserId or 0
	if murdererAvatarId ~= HubState.LastMurdererAvatarId then
		HubState.LastMurdererAvatarId = murdererAvatarId
		UpdateRoleAvatar(HubState.MurdererAvatar, HubState.CurrentMurderer, "Murderer")
	end
	if sheriffAvatarId ~= HubState.LastSheriffAvatarId then
		HubState.LastSheriffAvatarId = sheriffAvatarId
		UpdateRoleAvatar(HubState.SheriffAvatar, HubState.CurrentSheriff, "Sheriff")
	end
	HubState.MurdererRoleLabel.Text = "Murderer: " .. FormatRolePlayer(HubState.CurrentMurderer)
	HubState.SheriffRoleLabel.Text = "Sheriff: " .. FormatRolePlayer(HubState.CurrentSheriff)
	UpdateRoleHighlights()
end

ThemeObjects.ClearMM2Roles = function()
	HubState.CurrentMurderer = nil
	HubState.CurrentSheriff = nil
	ThemeObjects.RefreshMM2RoleDisplay()
end

local function FindRoleHolder(toolName)
	for _, targetPlayer in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
		if PlayerHasRoleTool(targetPlayer, toolName) then return targetPlayer end
	end
	return nil
end

ThemeObjects.ApplyMM2Roles = function(murderer, sheriff, source)
	if source then HubState.MM2RoleSource = source end
	if murderer ~= HubState.CurrentMurderer or sheriff ~= HubState.CurrentSheriff then
		HubState.CurrentMurderer = murderer
		HubState.CurrentSheriff = sheriff
		ThemeObjects.RefreshMM2RoleDisplay()
	end
	return murderer, sheriff
end

ThemeObjects.ResolveMM2RolePlayer = function(...)
	local seen = {}
	local function playerFromText(text)
		if type(text) ~= "string" or text == "" then return nil end
		local lowerText = text:lower()
		for _, targetPlayer in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
			local name = targetPlayer.Name:lower()
			local displayName = (targetPlayer.DisplayName or targetPlayer.Name):lower()
			if lowerText == name or lowerText == displayName or lowerText:find(name, 1, true) or lowerText:find(displayName, 1, true) then
				return targetPlayer
			end
		end
		return nil
	end
	local function resolve(value, depth)
		if depth > 4 or value == nil then return nil end
		local valueType = typeof(value)
		if valueType == "Instance" then
			if value:IsA("Player") then return value end
			if value:IsA("ObjectValue") then return resolve(value.Value, depth + 1) end
			if value:IsA("StringValue") then return playerFromText(tostring(value.Value)) end
			if value:IsA("IntValue") or value:IsA("NumberValue") then
				for _, targetPlayer in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
					if targetPlayer.UserId == value.Value then return targetPlayer end
				end
			end
			if value:IsA("TextLabel") or value:IsA("TextButton") then return playerFromText(value.Text) end
			return playerFromText(value.Name)
		elseif valueType == "string" then
			return playerFromText(value)
		elseif valueType == "number" then
			for _, targetPlayer in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
				if targetPlayer.UserId == value then return targetPlayer end
			end
		elseif valueType == "table" and not seen[value] then
			seen[value] = true
			for key, childValue in pairs(value) do
				local found = resolve(childValue, depth + 1) or resolve(key, depth + 1)
				if found then return found end
			end
		end
		return nil
	end
	for _, value in ipairs({...}) do
		local found = resolve(value, 0)
		if found then return found end
	end
	return nil
end

ThemeObjects.SetMM2RoleFromClue = function(roleName, ...)
	local targetPlayer = ThemeObjects.ResolveMM2RolePlayer(...)
	if not targetPlayer then return false end
	local murderer = HubState.CurrentMurderer
	local sheriff = HubState.CurrentSheriff
	if roleName == "Murderer" then
		murderer = targetPlayer
	elseif roleName == "Sheriff" then
		sheriff = targetPlayer
	else
		return false
	end
	HubState.LastMM2RemoteRoleAt = os.clock()
	ThemeObjects.ApplyMM2Roles(murderer, sheriff, "Remote")
	return true
end

ThemeObjects.MM2PlayerDataLooksUseful = function(playerData)
	if type(playerData) ~= "table" then return false end
	local matchedPlayers = 0
	local sawRole = false
	for playerName, roundData in pairs(playerData) do
		if type(playerName) == "string" and type(roundData) == "table" and Players:FindFirstChild(playerName) then
			matchedPlayers += 1
			if type(rawget(roundData, "Role")) == "string" then
				sawRole = true
			end
			if matchedPlayers >= 2 and sawRole then
				return true
			end
		end
	end
	return matchedPlayers >= 1 and sawRole
end

ThemeObjects.ApplyMM2RolesFromPlayerData = function(playerData)
	if not ThemeObjects.MM2PlayerDataLooksUseful(playerData) then return false end
	local murderer = nil
	local sheriff = nil
	for playerName, roundData in pairs(playerData) do
		if type(playerName) == "string" and type(roundData) == "table" then
			local targetPlayer = Players:FindFirstChild(playerName)
			local roleName = rawget(roundData, "Role")
			if targetPlayer and roleName == "Murderer" then
				murderer = targetPlayer
			elseif targetPlayer and (roleName == "Sheriff" or roleName == "Hero") then
				sheriff = targetPlayer
			end
		end
	end
	HubState.LastMM2RemoteRoleAt = os.clock()
	ThemeObjects.ApplyMM2Roles(murderer, sheriff, "Memory")
	return true
end

ThemeObjects.RefreshMM2RolesFromMemory = function()
	if os.clock() - (HubState.LastMM2MemoryScan or 0) < 1 then return false end
	HubState.LastMM2MemoryScan = os.clock()
	if type(HubState.MM2MemoryRoundSource) == "table" then
		local cachedPlayerData = rawget(HubState.MM2MemoryRoundSource, "PlayerData")
		if ThemeObjects.ApplyMM2RolesFromPlayerData(cachedPlayerData or HubState.MM2MemoryRoundSource) then
			return true
		end
		HubState.MM2MemoryRoundSource = nil
	end
	local getgcFunction = type(getgc) == "function" and getgc or nil
	if not getgcFunction then return false end
	local success, objects = pcall(getgcFunction, true)
	if not success or type(objects) ~= "table" then return false end

	for _, object in ipairs(objects) do
		if type(object) == "table" then
			local playerData = rawget(object, "PlayerData")
			if ThemeObjects.ApplyMM2RolesFromPlayerData(playerData) then
				HubState.MM2MemoryRoundSource = object
				return true
			end
			if ThemeObjects.MM2PlayerDataLooksUseful(object) and ThemeObjects.ApplyMM2RolesFromPlayerData(object) then
				HubState.MM2MemoryRoundSource = object
				return true
			end
		end
	end
	return false
end

ThemeObjects.EnsureMM2RoleClueListeners = function()
	if HubState.MM2RoleClueListenersStarted then return end
	local replicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
	local remotes = replicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("Remotes")
	local extras = remotes and remotes:FindFirstChild("Extras")
	local setMurderer = extras and extras:FindFirstChild("SetMurderer")
	local setSheriff = extras and extras:FindFirstChild("SetSheriff")
	if not setMurderer and not setSheriff then return end
	HubState.MM2RoleClueListenersStarted = true
	if setMurderer and setMurderer:IsA("RemoteEvent") then
		HubState.Connections.MM2SetMurdererClue = setMurderer.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(...)
			ThemeObjects.SetMM2RoleFromClue("Murderer", ...)
		end)
	end
	if setSheriff and setSheriff:IsA("RemoteEvent") then
		HubState.Connections.MM2SetSheriffClue = setSheriff.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(...)
			ThemeObjects.SetMM2RoleFromClue("Sheriff", ...)
		end)
	end
end

ThemeObjects.RefreshMM2RolesFromRemote = function()
	if ThemeObjects.RefreshMM2RolesFromMemory and ThemeObjects.RefreshMM2RolesFromMemory() then return end
	if ThemeObjects.EnsureMM2RoleClueListeners then ThemeObjects.EnsureMM2RoleClueListeners() end
end

task.spawn(function()
	for _ = 1, 40 do
		if ThemeObjects.EnsureMM2RoleClueListeners then ThemeObjects.EnsureMM2RoleClueListeners() end
		if HubState.MM2RoleClueListenersStarted then break end
		task.wait(0.25)
	end
end)

ThemeObjects.RefreshMM2RolesFromTools = function()
	local murderer = FindRoleHolder("Knife")
	local sheriff = FindRoleHolder("Gun")
	if not murderer and not sheriff and HubState.MM2RoleSource == "Remote" and os.clock() - (HubState.LastMM2RemoteRoleAt or 0) < 45 then
		return HubState.CurrentMurderer, HubState.CurrentSheriff
	end
	return ThemeObjects.ApplyMM2Roles(murderer, sheriff, "Tools")
end

HubState.Connections.MM2ToolRoleScanner = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
	local mm2PageActive = HubState.SelectedGame == "MM2" or (HubState.MM2Page and HubState.MM2Page.Visible)
	local needsScan = mm2PageActive or HubState.MM2ESPEnabled or HubState.MurdererRoleESPEnabled or HubState.SheriffRoleESPEnabled or HubState.KillEnabled or HubState.AutoShootEnabled or HubState.ESPEnabled or ThemeObjects.DeepESP.Enabled
	if not needsScan then return end
	local now = os.clock()
	if now - (HubState.LastMM2ToolRoleScan or 0) < 0.25 then return end
	HubState.LastMM2ToolRoleScan = now
	ThemeObjects.RefreshMM2RolesFromTools()
	if now - (HubState.LastMM2RoleRemoteScan or 0) >= 0.8 then
		HubState.LastMM2RoleRemoteScan = now
		ThemeObjects.RefreshMM2RolesFromRemote()
	end
end)

local function RestoreKillHitboxes()
	for part, original in pairs(HubState.KillHitboxOriginals) do
		if part and part.Parent then
			part.Size = original.Size
			part.Transparency = original.Transparency
			part.CanCollide = original.CanCollide
			part.CanTouch = original.CanTouch
			part.Massless = original.Massless
		end
	end
	HubState.KillHitboxOriginals = {}
end

local function GetLocalKnife()
	local character = Player.Character
	local backpack = Player:FindFirstChild("Backpack")
	local knife = character and character:FindFirstChild("Knife")
	if not knife and backpack then knife = backpack:FindFirstChild("Knife") end
	return knife and knife:IsA("Tool") and knife or nil
end

local function SetKillEnabled(enabled)
	HubState.KillEnabled = enabled
	HubState.KillToggle.Text = enabled and "On" or "Off"
	HubState.KillTitle.TextColor3 = enabled and Color3.fromRGB(255, 80, 80) or InactiveTextColor()
	if enabled and ThemeObjects.RefreshMM2RolesFromRemote then ThemeObjects.RefreshMM2RolesFromRemote() end
	if not enabled then RestoreKillHitboxes() end
end

HubState.KillToggle.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
	PlayClick()
	SetKillEnabled(not HubState.KillEnabled)
end)

HubState.Connections.KillAll = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
	if not HubState.KillEnabled then return end
	local knife = GetLocalKnife()
	local character = Player.Character
	local humanoid = character and character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
	if HubState.CurrentMurderer ~= Player or not knife or not humanoid or humanoid.Health <= 0 then
		RestoreKillHitboxes()
		return
	end

	if knife.Parent ~= character then
		pcall(function() humanoid:EquipTool(knife) end)
	end

	local aliveTargets = {}
	local priorityRoot = nil
	if HubState.CurrentSheriff and HubState.CurrentSheriff ~= Player then
		local sheriffCharacter = HubState.CurrentSheriff.Character
		local sheriffHumanoid = sheriffCharacter and sheriffCharacter:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
		local sheriffRoot = sheriffCharacter and sheriffCharacter:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
		if sheriffHumanoid and sheriffHumanoid.Health > 0 and sheriffRoot then priorityRoot = sheriffRoot end
	end

	if priorityRoot then
		for part, original in pairs(HubState.KillHitboxOriginals) do
			if part ~= priorityRoot then
				if part and part.Parent then
					part.Size = original.Size
					part.Transparency = original.Transparency
					part.CanCollide = original.CanCollide
					part.CanTouch = original.CanTouch
					part.Massless = original.Massless
				end
				HubState.KillHitboxOriginals[part] = nil
			end
		end
	end

	for _, targetPlayer in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
		if targetPlayer ~= Player then
			local targetCharacter = targetPlayer.Character
			local targetHumanoid = targetCharacter and targetCharacter:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
			local targetRoot = targetCharacter and targetCharacter:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
			if targetHumanoid and targetHumanoid.Health > 0 and targetRoot and (not priorityRoot or targetRoot == priorityRoot) then
				table.insert(aliveTargets, targetRoot)
				if not HubState.KillHitboxOriginals[targetRoot] then
					HubState.KillHitboxOriginals[targetRoot] = {
						Size = targetRoot.Size,
						Transparency = targetRoot.Transparency,
						CanCollide = targetRoot.CanCollide,
						CanTouch = targetRoot.CanTouch,
						Massless = targetRoot.Massless,
					}
				end
				targetRoot.Size = type(firetouchinterest) == "function" and Vector3.new(50, 50, 50) or Vector3.new(2048, 2048, 2048)
				targetRoot.Transparency = 1
				targetRoot.CanCollide = false
				targetRoot.CanTouch = true
				targetRoot.Massless = true
			end
		end
	end

	local now = os.clock()
	if now - HubState.LastKnifeSwing >= 0.1 then
		HubState.LastKnifeSwing = now
		pcall(function() knife:Activate() end)
		if #aliveTargets > 0 then
			HubState.StabTargetIndex = (HubState.StabTargetIndex % #aliveTargets) + 1
			local targetRoot = aliveTargets[HubState.StabTargetIndex]
			local knifeHandle = knife:FindFirstChild("Handle") or knife:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart")
			if knifeHandle and type(firetouchinterest) == "function" then
				task.spawn(function()
					pcall(function()
						firetouchinterest(knifeHandle, targetRoot, 0)
						task.wait(0.03)
						firetouchinterest(knifeHandle, targetRoot, 1)
					end)
				end)
			end
		end
	end
end)

do
	local autoShootTitle = Instance.new("TextLabel")
	autoShootTitle.Size = UDim2.new(0, 56, 0, 17)
	autoShootTitle.Position = UDim2.new(0, 176, 0, 70)

	autoShootTitle.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold

	autoShootTitle.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
	autoShootTitle.Parent = HubState.MM2Page
	table.insert(ThemeObjects.Texts, autoShootTitle)

	local autoShootToggle = Instance.new("TextButton")
	autoShootToggle.Size = UDim2.new(0, 32, 0, 17)
	autoShootToggle.Position = UDim2.new(0, 240, 0, 70)
	autoShootToggle.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 68)
	autoShootToggle.BackgroundTransparency = 0.8
	autoShootToggle.BorderSizePixel = 0
	autoShootToggle.Text = "Off"
	autoShootToggle.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
	autoShootToggle.Parent = HubState.MM2Page
	table.insert(ThemeObjects.Backgrounds, autoShootToggle)
	table.insert(ThemeObjects.Texts, autoShootToggle)
	Instance.new("UICorner", autoShootToggle).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4)

	-- Larger MM2 controls live in a dedicated scrolling area below the role reveal.
	local MM2ControlsScroll = Instance.new("ScrollingFrame")
	MM2ControlsScroll.Name = "MM2ControlsScroll"
	MM2ControlsScroll.Size = UDim2.new(1, -12, 1, -74)
	MM2ControlsScroll.Position = UDim2.new(0, 6, 0, 72)
	MM2ControlsScroll.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	MM2ControlsScroll.BorderSizePixel = 0
	MM2ControlsScroll.ScrollBarThickness = 3
	MM2ControlsScroll.ScrollBarImageColor3 = AccentColor
	MM2ControlsScroll.ScrollingDirection = Enum.ScrollingDirection.Y
	MM2ControlsScroll.ElasticBehavior = Enum.ElasticBehavior.Never
	MM2ControlsScroll.VerticalScrollBarInset = Enum.ScrollBarInset.ScrollBar
	MM2ControlsScroll.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 206)
	MM2ControlsScroll.ClipsDescendants = true
	MM2ControlsScroll.Parent = HubState.MM2Page

	local function CreateMM2ControlRow(name, widthScale, widthOffset, xScale, xOffset, y, height)
		local row = Instance.new("Frame")
		row.Name = name
		row.Size = UDim2.new(widthScale, widthOffset, 0, height)
		row.Position = UDim2.new(xScale, xOffset, 0, y)
		row.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(240, 240, 240)
		row.BackgroundTransparency = 0.92
		row.BorderSizePixel = 0
		row.Parent = MM2ControlsScroll
		table.insert(ThemeObjects.Backgrounds, row)
		Instance.new("UICorner", row).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)
		return row
	end

	local mm2ESPRow = CreateMM2ControlRow("MM2ESPRow", 1, -8, 0, 4, -44, 38)
	mm2ESPRow.Visible = false
	local stabRow = CreateMM2ControlRow("AutoStabRow", 1, -8, 0, 4, 4, 38)
	local shootRow = CreateMM2ControlRow("AutoShootRow", 1, -8, 0, 4, 48, 38)
	local gunRow = CreateMM2ControlRow("AutoGunRow", 1, -8, 0, 4, 92, 38)
	local coinRow = CreateMM2ControlRow("CoinFarmRow", 1, -8, 0, 4, 136, 38)

	local function PlaceMM2Control(title, toggle, row, fullWidth)
		title.Size = fullWidth and UDim2.new(0, 130, 0, 24) or UDim2.new(0, 82, 0, 22)
		title.Position = fullWidth and UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 7) or UDim2.new(0, 8, 0, 7)
		title.TextSize = fullWidth and 11 or 10
		title.Parent = row
		toggle.Size = fullWidth and UDim2.new(0, 44, 0, 22) or UDim2.new(0, 38, 0, 20)
		toggle.Position = fullWidth and UDim2.new(1, -52, 0, 8) or UDim2.new(1, -44, 0, 8)
		toggle.TextSize = 9
		toggle.Parent = row
	end

	HubState.MM2ESPTitle = Instance.new("TextLabel")
	HubState.MM2ESPTitle.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	HubState.MM2ESPTitle.Text = "Merged ESP:"
	HubState.MM2ESPTitle.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
	HubState.MM2ESPTitle.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
	HubState.MM2ESPTitle.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
	table.insert(ThemeObjects.Texts, HubState.MM2ESPTitle)
	HubState.MM2ESPToggle = Instance.new("TextButton")
	HubState.MM2ESPToggle.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 68)
	HubState.MM2ESPToggle.BackgroundTransparency = 0.8
	HubState.MM2ESPToggle.BorderSizePixel = 0
	HubState.MM2ESPToggle.Text = "Off"
	HubState.MM2ESPToggle.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
	table.insert(ThemeObjects.Backgrounds, HubState.MM2ESPToggle)
	table.insert(ThemeObjects.Texts, HubState.MM2ESPToggle)
	Instance.new("UICorner", HubState.MM2ESPToggle).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4)
	PlaceMM2Control(HubState.MM2ESPTitle, HubState.MM2ESPToggle, mm2ESPRow)
	HubState.MM2ESPToggle.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		PlayClick()
		ThemeObjects.SetMM2ESP(not HubState.MM2ESPEnabled)
	end)
	table.insert(ThemeObjects.StateTexts, {Object = HubState.MM2ESPTitle, IsEnabled = function() return HubState.MM2ESPEnabled end})
	PlaceMM2Control(HubState.KillTitle, HubState.KillToggle, stabRow)
	PlaceMM2Control(autoShootTitle, autoShootToggle, shootRow)
	PlaceMM2Control(HubState.AutoGunTitle, HubState.AutoGunToggle, gunRow)
	PlaceMM2Control(HubState.CoinFarmTitle, HubState.CoinFarmToggle, coinRow)
	HubState.CoinFarmStatus.Visible = false
	HubState.CoinFarmStatus.Parent = coinRow
	ThemeObjects.AddFeatureKeybind({Name = "Auto Gun", Storage = "MM2AutoGun", Parent = gunRow, Toggle = HubState.AutoGunToggle, Get = function() return LoadKeybind("MM2AutoGun") end, Set = function(key) SaveKeybind("MM2AutoGun", key) end, Action = function()
		HubState.AutoGunPickupEnabled = not HubState.AutoGunPickupEnabled
		HubState.AutoGunToggle.Text = HubState.AutoGunPickupEnabled and "On" or "Off"
		HubState.AutoGunTitle.TextColor3 = HubState.AutoGunPickupEnabled and AccentColor or InactiveTextColor()
		HubState.LastGunDrop = nil
	end})
	ThemeObjects.AddFeatureKeybind({Name = "Auto Stab", Storage = "MM2AutoStab", Parent = stabRow, Toggle = HubState.KillToggle, Get = function() return LoadKeybind("MM2AutoStab") end, Set = function(key) SaveKeybind("MM2AutoStab", key) end, Action = function()
		SetKillEnabled(not HubState.KillEnabled)
	end})
	ThemeObjects.AddFeatureKeybind({Name = "Coin Farm", Storage = "MM2CoinFarm", Parent = coinRow, Toggle = HubState.CoinFarmToggle, Get = function() return LoadKeybind("MM2CoinFarm") end, Set = function(key) SaveKeybind("MM2CoinFarm", key) end, Action = ToggleCoinFarm})

	local autoShootEnabled = false
	local lastGunFired = 0
	local shotPending = false
	local AutoShootConfirmWindow = 0.05
	local AutoShootLeadTime = 0.06

	local function GetLocalGun()
		local character = Player.Character
		local backpack = Player:FindFirstChild("Backpack")
		local gun = character and character:FindFirstChild("Gun")
		if not gun and backpack then gun = backpack:FindFirstChild("Gun") end
		return gun and gun:IsA("Tool") and gun or nil
	end

	local function HasClearGunLine(originPosition, targetCharacter, targetPart)
		local ignoreList = {Player.Character}
		for _, passthrough in ipairs(game:GetService("CollectionService"):GetTagged("WeaponPassthrough")) do
			table.insert(ignoreList, passthrough)
		end
		local raycastParams = RaycastParams.new()
		raycastParams.FilterType = Enum.RaycastFilterType.Exclude
		raycastParams.IgnoreWater = true
		raycastParams.FilterDescendantsInstances = ignoreList
		local direction = targetPart.Position - originPosition

		while true do
			local result = workspace:Raycast(originPosition, direction, raycastParams)
			if not result then return true end
			if result.Instance and result.Instance:IsDescendantOf(targetCharacter) then return true end
			if result.Instance and result.Instance.Transparency == 1 then
				table.insert(ignoreList, result.Instance)
				raycastParams.FilterDescendantsInstances = ignoreList
			else
				return false
			end
		end
	end

	local function SetAutoShootEnabled(enabled)
		autoShootEnabled = enabled
		HubState.AutoShootEnabled = enabled
		autoShootToggle.Text = enabled and "On" or "Off"
		autoShootTitle.TextColor3 = enabled and Color3.fromRGB(90, 150, 255) or InactiveTextColor()
		if enabled and ThemeObjects.RefreshMM2RolesFromTools then ThemeObjects.RefreshMM2RolesFromTools() end
		if enabled and ThemeObjects.RefreshMM2RolesFromRemote then ThemeObjects.RefreshMM2RolesFromRemote() end
		if enabled and HubState.AutoLockEnabled then ToggleAutoLock() end
	end

	autoShootToggle.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		PlayClick()
		SetAutoShootEnabled(not autoShootEnabled)
	end)

	table.insert(ThemeObjects.StateTexts, {Object = autoShootTitle, IsEnabled = function() return autoShootEnabled end})
	ThemeObjects.AddFeatureKeybind({Name = "Auto Shoot", Storage = "MM2AutoShoot", Parent = shootRow, Toggle = autoShootToggle, Get = function() return LoadKeybind("MM2AutoShoot") end, Set = function(key) SaveKeybind("MM2AutoShoot", key) end, Action = function()
		SetAutoShootEnabled(not autoShootEnabled)
	end})

	HubState.Connections.AutoShoot = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
		if not autoShootEnabled then return end
		if HubState.AutoLockEnabled then ToggleAutoLock() end
		if ThemeObjects.RefreshMM2RolesFromTools and os.clock() - (HubState.LastMM2AutoShootRoleScan or 0) >= 0.25 then
			HubState.LastMM2AutoShootRoleScan = os.clock()
			ThemeObjects.RefreshMM2RolesFromTools()
		end
		if HubState.CurrentSheriff ~= Player or not HubState.CurrentMurderer or HubState.CurrentMurderer == Player then return end

		local gun = GetLocalGun()
		local character = Player.Character
		local humanoid = character and character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
		local targetCharacter = HubState.CurrentMurderer.Character
		local targetHumanoid = targetCharacter and targetCharacter:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
		local targetPart = targetCharacter and (targetCharacter:FindFirstChild("UpperTorso") or targetCharacter:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or targetCharacter:FindFirstChild("Head"))
		if not gun or not humanoid or humanoid.Health <= 0 or not targetHumanoid or targetHumanoid.Health <= 0 or not targetPart then return end

		if gun.Parent ~= character then
			pcall(function() humanoid:EquipTool(gun) end)
			return
		end
		if shotPending or os.clock() - lastGunFired < 0.75 then return end
		local localRoot = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
		local raycastAttachment = localRoot and localRoot:FindFirstChild("GunRaycastAttachment")
		local shootRemote = gun:FindFirstChild("Shoot")
		if not shootRemote or not shootRemote:IsA("RemoteEvent") then return end
		local shotOrigin = raycastAttachment and raycastAttachment.WorldCFrame or nil
		if not shotOrigin or not HasClearGunLine(shotOrigin.Position, targetCharacter, targetPart) then return end

		-- Take a second movement sample before firing. Sharp reversals cancel this
		-- attempt, preventing a quick juke from baiting a stale shot.
		local confirmedMurderer = HubState.CurrentMurderer
		local firstPosition = targetPart.Position
		local firstVelocity = targetPart.AssemblyLinearVelocity
		shotPending = true
		task.delay(AutoShootConfirmWindow, function()
			shotPending = false
			if not autoShootEnabled or HubState.CurrentSheriff ~= Player or HubState.CurrentMurderer ~= confirmedMurderer then return end

			local freshCharacter = Player.Character
			local freshHumanoid = freshCharacter and freshCharacter:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
			local freshTargetCharacter = confirmedMurderer and confirmedMurderer.Character
			local freshTargetHumanoid = freshTargetCharacter and freshTargetCharacter:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
			local freshTargetPart = freshTargetCharacter and (freshTargetCharacter:FindFirstChild("UpperTorso") or freshTargetCharacter:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or freshTargetCharacter:FindFirstChild("Head"))
			local freshGun = GetLocalGun()
			if not freshCharacter or not freshHumanoid or freshHumanoid.Health <= 0 or not freshTargetHumanoid or freshTargetHumanoid.Health <= 0 or not freshTargetPart or not freshGun then return end
			if freshGun.Parent ~= freshCharacter then return end

			local freshRoot = freshCharacter:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
			local freshAttachment = freshRoot and freshRoot:FindFirstChild("GunRaycastAttachment")
			local freshRemote = freshGun:FindFirstChild("Shoot")
			local freshOrigin = freshAttachment and freshAttachment.WorldCFrame
			if not freshOrigin or not freshRemote or not freshRemote:IsA("RemoteEvent") then return end

			local currentPosition = freshTargetPart.Position
			local currentVelocity = freshTargetPart.AssemblyLinearVelocity
			local expectedPosition = firstPosition + firstVelocity * AutoShootConfirmWindow
			local movementError = (currentPosition - expectedPosition).Magnitude
			local velocityChange = (currentVelocity - firstVelocity).Magnitude
			if movementError > 6.0 or velocityChange > 60 then return end
			if not HasClearGunLine(freshOrigin.Position, freshTargetCharacter, freshTargetPart) then return end

			local leadOffset = currentVelocity * AutoShootLeadTime
			if leadOffset.Magnitude > 6 then leadOffset = leadOffset.Unit * 6 end
			local targetCFrame = CFrame.new(currentPosition + leadOffset)
			lastGunFired = os.clock()
			pcall(function() freshRemote:FireServer(freshOrigin, targetCFrame) end)
		end)
	end)
end
