-- Movement Logic
ThemeObjects.BindingConnections = {}
local function SetupBinding(button, type)
	button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		PlayClick()
		if ThemeObjects.BindingConnections[type] then
			ThemeObjects.BindingConnections[type]:Disconnect()
			ThemeObjects.BindingConnections[type] = nil
		end
		button.Text = "..."
		if type == "Speed" then HubState.IsBindingSpeed = true
		elseif type == "Noclip" then HubState.IsBindingNoclip = true
		elseif type == "Fly" then HubState.IsBindingFly = true
		elseif type == "FreeCam" then ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Binding = true
		elseif type == "AutoLock" then HubState.IsBindingAutoLock = true
		elseif type == "ESP" then HubState.IsBindingESP = true end
		
		local conn
		conn = UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, processed)
			if processed then return end
			if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Keyboard then
				local selectedKey = input.KeyCode
				if selectedKey == Enum.KeyCode.Backspace or selectedKey == Enum.KeyCode.Delete then
					selectedKey = Enum.KeyCode.Unknown
				end
				if type == "Speed" then HubState.SpeedKeybind = selectedKey; HubState.IsBindingSpeed = false
				elseif type == "Noclip" then HubState.NoclipKeybind = selectedKey; HubState.IsBindingNoclip = false
				elseif type == "Fly" then HubState.FlyKeybind = selectedKey; HubState.IsBindingFly = false
				elseif type == "FreeCam" then ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Keybind = selectedKey; ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Binding = false
				elseif type == "AutoLock" then HubState.AutoLockKeybind = selectedKey; HubState.IsBindingAutoLock = false
				elseif type == "ESP" then HubState.ESPKeybind = selectedKey; HubState.IsBindingESP = false end
				
				SaveKeybind(type, selectedKey)
				button.Text = KeybindText(selectedKey)
				ThemeObjects.BindingConnections[type] = nil
				conn:Disconnect()
			end
		end)
		ThemeObjects.BindingConnections[type] = conn
	end)
end

SetupBinding(HubState.SpeedBindBtn, "Speed")
SetupBinding(HubState.NoclipBindBtn, "Noclip")
SetupBinding(HubState.FlyBindBtn, "Fly")
SetupBinding(ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Bind, "FreeCam")
SetupBinding(HubState.AutoLockBindBtn, "AutoLock")
SetupBinding(HubState.ESPBindBtn, "ESP")
ThemeObjects.AddFeatureKeybind({Name = "Auto Lock", Storage = "AutoLock", Button = HubState.AutoLockBindBtn, Get = function() return HubState.AutoLockKeybind end, Set = function(key) HubState.AutoLockKeybind = key; SaveKeybind("AutoLock", key); if HubState.AutoLockBindBtn then HubState.AutoLockBindBtn.Text = KeybindText(key) end end, Action = ToggleAutoLock})
ThemeObjects.AddFeatureKeybind({Name = "Fly", Storage = "Fly", Button = HubState.FlyBindBtn, Get = function() return HubState.FlyKeybind end, Set = function(key) HubState.FlyKeybind = key; SaveKeybind("Fly", key); if HubState.FlyBindBtn then HubState.FlyBindBtn.Text = KeybindText(key) end end, Action = ToggleFly})
ThemeObjects.AddFeatureKeybind({Name = "Free Cam", Storage = "FreeCam", Button = ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Bind, Get = function() return ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Keybind end, Set = function(key) ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Keybind = key; SaveKeybind("FreeCam", key); if ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Bind then ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Bind.Text = KeybindText(key) end end, Action = function() ThemeObjects.FreeCam.ToggleState() end})
ThemeObjects.AddFeatureKeybind({Name = "No Clip", Storage = "Noclip", Button = HubState.NoclipBindBtn, Get = function() return HubState.NoclipKeybind end, Set = function(key) HubState.NoclipKeybind = key; SaveKeybind("Noclip", key); if HubState.NoclipBindBtn then HubState.NoclipBindBtn.Text = KeybindText(key) end end, Action = ToggleNoclip})
ThemeObjects.AddFeatureKeybind({Name = "Outline ESP", Storage = "ESP", Button = HubState.ESPBindBtn, Get = function() return HubState.ESPKeybind end, Set = function(key) HubState.ESPKeybind = key; SaveKeybind("ESP", key); if HubState.ESPBindBtn then HubState.ESPBindBtn.Text = KeybindText(key) end end, Action = ToggleESP})
ThemeObjects.AddFeatureKeybind({Name = "Speed", Storage = "Speed", Button = HubState.SpeedBindBtn, Get = function() return HubState.SpeedKeybind end, Set = function(key) HubState.SpeedKeybind = key; SaveKeybind("Speed", key); if HubState.SpeedBindBtn then HubState.SpeedBindBtn.Text = KeybindText(key) end end, Action = ToggleSpeed})

local function ToggleSpeed()
	HubState.SpeedEnabled = not HubState.SpeedEnabled
	HubState.SpeedToggleBtn.Text = HubState.SpeedEnabled and "On" or "Off"
	HubState.SpeedTitle.TextColor3 = HubState.SpeedEnabled and AccentColor or InactiveTextColor()
end
HubState.SpeedToggleBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() PlayClick() ToggleSpeed() end)

local function ToggleNoclip()
	HubState.NoclipEnabled = not HubState.NoclipEnabled
	HubState.NoclipToggleBtn.Text = HubState.NoclipEnabled and "On" or "Off"
	HubState.NoclipTitle.TextColor3 = HubState.NoclipEnabled and AccentColor or InactiveTextColor()
end
HubState.NoclipToggleBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() PlayClick() ToggleNoclip() end)

HubState.Connections.NoclipLoop = RunService.Stepped:Connect(function()
	if HubState.NoclipEnabled and Player.Character then
		for _, part in pairs(Player.Character:GetDescendants()) do
			if part:IsA("BasePart") and part.CanCollide then part.CanCollide = false end
		end
	end
end)

function ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Enable()
	if ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Enabled then return end
	local camera = workspace.CurrentCamera
	if not camera then return end
	ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Enabled = true
	ThemeObjects.FreeCam.OriginalType = camera.CameraType
	ThemeObjects.FreeCam.OriginalSubject = camera.CameraSubject
	ThemeObjects.FreeCam.OriginalCFrame = camera.CFrame
	ThemeObjects.FreeCam.OriginalFocus = camera.Focus
	ThemeObjects.FreeCam.OriginalMouseBehavior = UserInputService.MouseBehavior
	ThemeObjects.FreeCam.OriginalMouseIcon = UserInputService.MouseIconEnabled
	ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Position = camera.CFrame.Position
	ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Pitch, ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Yaw = camera.CFrame:ToOrientation()
	camera.CameraType = Enum.CameraType.Scriptable
	local character = Player.Character
	local humanoid = character and character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
	local root = character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
	if humanoid then humanoid:Move(Vector3.zero) end
	if root then root.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.zero root.AssemblyAngularVelocity = Vector3.zero end
	ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Toggle.Text = "On"
	ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Title.TextColor3 = AccentColor
	game:GetService("ContextActionService"):BindActionAtPriority(
		"HqydeuFreeCamSink",
		function() return Enum.ContextActionResult.Sink end,
		false,
		Enum.ContextActionPriority.High.Value + 100,
		Enum.KeyCode.W, Enum.KeyCode.A, Enum.KeyCode.S, Enum.KeyCode.D,
		Enum.KeyCode.Q, Enum.KeyCode.E, Enum.KeyCode.LeftShift
	)
end

function ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Disable()
	if not ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Enabled then return end
	ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Enabled = false
	game:GetService("ContextActionService"):UnbindAction("HqydeuFreeCamSink")
	-- Always release the RMB camera lock. Restoring a captured LockCenter state can
	-- leave the cursor pinned after Free Cam is turned off.
	UserInputService.MouseBehavior = Enum.MouseBehavior.Default
	UserInputService.MouseIconEnabled = true
	local camera = workspace.CurrentCamera
	if camera then
		camera.CameraType = ThemeObjects.FreeCam.OriginalType or Enum.CameraType.Custom
		local character = Player.Character
		local humanoid = character and character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
		camera.CameraSubject = humanoid or ThemeObjects.FreeCam.OriginalSubject
		if ThemeObjects.FreeCam.OriginalCFrame then camera.CFrame = ThemeObjects.FreeCam.OriginalCFrame end
		if ThemeObjects.FreeCam.OriginalFocus then camera.Focus = ThemeObjects.FreeCam.OriginalFocus end
	end
	ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Toggle.Text = "Off"
	ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Title.TextColor3 = InactiveTextColor()
	task.defer(function()
		-- Apply once more after Roblox's camera controller finishes this frame.
		if not ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Enabled then
			UserInputService.MouseBehavior = Enum.MouseBehavior.Default
			UserInputService.MouseIconEnabled = true
		end
	end)
end

function ThemeObjects.FreeCam.ToggleState()
	if ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Enabled then ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Disable() else ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Enable() end
end

ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Toggle.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() PlayClick() ThemeObjects.FreeCam.ToggleState() end)
HubState.Connections.FreeCam = RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function(deltaTime)
	if not ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Enabled then return end
	local camera = workspace.CurrentCamera
	if not camera then return end
	ThemeObjects.FreeCam.FocusedTextBox = nil
	pcall(function() ThemeObjects.FreeCam.FocusedTextBox = UserInputService:GetFocusedTextBox() end)
	if ThemeObjects.FreeCam.FocusedTextBox then
		UserInputService.MouseBehavior = Enum.MouseBehavior.Default
		return
	end
	if UserInputService:IsMouseButtonPressed(Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton2) then
		UserInputService.MouseBehavior = Enum.MouseBehavior.LockCurrentPosition
		local mouseDelta = UserInputService:GetMouseDelta()
		ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Yaw = ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Yaw - mouseDelta.X * 0.01
		ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Pitch = math.clamp(ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Pitch - mouseDelta.Y * 0.01, math.rad(-89), math.rad(89))
	else
		UserInputService.MouseBehavior = Enum.MouseBehavior.Default
	end
	local rotation = CFrame.fromOrientation(ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Pitch, ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Yaw, 0)
	local movement = Vector3.zero
	if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.W) then movement = movement + rotation.LookVector end
	if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.S) then movement = movement - rotation.LookVector end
	if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.D) then movement = movement + rotation.RightVector end
	if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.A) then movement = movement - rotation.RightVector end
	if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.E) then movement = movement + Vector3.new(0, 1, 0) end
	if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.Q) then movement = movement - Vector3.new(0, 1, 0) end
	local speed = UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.LeftShift) and 120 or 40
	if movement.Magnitude > 0 then ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Position = ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Position + movement.Unit * speed * deltaTime end
	local cameraCFrame = CFrame.new(ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Position) * rotation
	camera.CFrame = cameraCFrame
	camera.Focus = cameraCFrame * CFrame.new(0, 0, -512)
end)

local function ToggleFly()
	HubState.FlyEnabled = not HubState.FlyEnabled
	HubState.FlyToggleBtn.Text = HubState.FlyEnabled and "On" or "Off"
	HubState.FlyTitle.TextColor3 = HubState.FlyEnabled and AccentColor or InactiveTextColor()
	local Character = Player.Character 
	local RootPart = Character and Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
	if HubState.FlyEnabled then
		if RootPart then
			HubState.BodyVelocity = Instance.new("BodyVelocity") HubState.BodyVelocity.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0) HubState.BodyVelocity.MaxForce = Vector3.new(math.huge, math.huge, math.huge) HubState.BodyVelocity.Parent = RootPart
			HubState.BodyGyro = Instance.new("BodyGyro") HubState.BodyGyro.P = 9e4 HubState.BodyGyro.MaxTorque = Vector3.new(9e9, 9e9, 9e9) HubState.BodyGyro.CFrame = RootPart.CFrame HubState.BodyGyro.Parent = RootPart
		end
	else
		if HubState.BodyVelocity then HubState.BodyVelocity:Destroy() HubState.BodyVelocity = nil end
		if HubState.BodyGyro then HubState.BodyGyro:Destroy() HubState.BodyGyro = nil end
		if RootPart then
			RootPart.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
			ThemeObjects.SetRootUpright(RootPart, RootPart.CFrame, RootPart.Position)
		end
	end
end
HubState.FlyToggleBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() PlayClick() ToggleFly() end)

local function GetClosestPlayerToMouse()
	local nearest = nil
	local lastDist = math.huge
	local Camera = workspace.CurrentCamera
	local MousePos = UserInputService:GetMouseLocation()
	for _, p in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
		if p ~= Player and p.Character and p.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") then
			local headPos, onScreen = Camera:WorldToViewportPoint(p.Character.Head.Position)
			if onScreen then
				local dist = (Vector2.new(headPos.X, headPos.Y) - MousePos).Magnitude
				if dist < lastDist then
					nearest = p
					lastDist = dist
				end
			end
		end
	end
	return nearest
end

-- Rendering Loop
HubState.Connections.MainLoop = RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
	local Character = Player.Character 
    local RootPart = Character and Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") 
    local Humanoid = Character and Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") 
    local Camera = workspace.CurrentCamera

    if HubState.SpeedEnabled and RootPart and Humanoid then
		local MoveDir = Humanoid.MoveDirection 
        if MoveDir.Magnitude > 0 then 
            RootPart.CFrame = RootPart.CFrame + (MoveDir * (HubState.CurrentCFrameSpeed / 10)) 
        end
	end
    
	if HubState.FlyEnabled and RootPart and HubState.BodyGyro then
		local MoveDir = Vector3.new(0,0,0)
		if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.W) then MoveDir = MoveDir + Camera.CFrame.LookVector end
		if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.S) then MoveDir = MoveDir - Camera.CFrame.LookVector end
		if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.A) then MoveDir = MoveDir - Camera.CFrame.RightVector end
		if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.D) then MoveDir = MoveDir + Camera.CFrame.RightVector end
		if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.Space) then MoveDir = MoveDir + Vector3.new(0,1,0) end
		if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.LeftShift) then MoveDir = MoveDir - Vector3.new(0,1,0) end
		if MoveDir.Magnitude > 0 then RootPart.CFrame = RootPart.CFrame + (MoveDir * (HubState.FlySpeed / 50)) end
		local _, yaw = Camera.CFrame:ToOrientation()
		HubState.BodyGyro.CFrame = CFrame.new(RootPart.Position) * CFrame.Angles(0, yaw, 0)
		RootPart.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
		RootPart.AssemblyAngularVelocity = Vector3.zero
	end
	
	if HubState.AutoLockEnabled and UserInputService:IsMouseButtonPressed(Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton2) and RootPart then
		local target = GetClosestPlayerToMouse()
		if target and target.Character and target.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") then
			Camera.CFrame = CFrame.lookAt(Camera.CFrame.Position, target.Character.Head.Position)
		end
	end

	local hasESPVisuals = next(ThemeObjects.ESPHighlights) ~= nil or next(ThemeObjects.ESPAdornments) ~= nil
	local needsPlayerMaintenance = HubState.AntiFlingEnabled or HubState.ESPEnabled or ThemeObjects.DeepESP.Enabled or hasESPVisuals
	if not needsPlayerMaintenance then return end
	local now = os.clock()
	local maintenanceInterval = HubState.AntiFlingEnabled and 0.05 or 0.12
	if now - (ThemeObjects.LastPlayerMaintenanceRefresh or 0) < maintenanceInterval then return end
	ThemeObjects.LastPlayerMaintenanceRefresh = now
	local refreshESPBody = ThemeObjects.DeepESP.Enabled and now - (ThemeObjects.LastESPBodyRefresh or 0) >= 0.18
	if refreshESPBody then ThemeObjects.LastESPBodyRefresh = now end
	local killerFolder = (HubState.ESPEnabled or ThemeObjects.DeepESP.Enabled) and workspace:FindFirstChild("KillerFolder") or nil
    for _, p in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
		local char = ThemeObjects.ResolveESPCharacter(p)
		local hum = char and char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
		local root = char and (char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or char:FindFirstChild("UpperTorso") or char:FindFirstChild("Torso") or char.PrimaryPart)
        if p ~= Player and char and root and hum then

			if HubState.AntiFlingEnabled and not HubState.Flinging then
				local dangerous = root.AssemblyLinearVelocity.Magnitude > 90 or root.AssemblyAngularVelocity.Magnitude > 40
				for _, part in ipairs(char:GetDescendants()) do
					if part:IsA("BasePart") then
						if dangerous then
							if HubState.AntiFlingOriginalCollision[part] == nil then
								HubState.AntiFlingOriginalCollision[part] = part.CanCollide
							end
							part.CanCollide = false
						elseif HubState.AntiFlingOriginalCollision[part] ~= nil then
							part.CanCollide = HubState.AntiFlingOriginalCollision[part]
							HubState.AntiFlingOriginalCollision[part] = nil
						end
					end
				end
			end
            
			local sharedESPEnabled = HubState.ESPEnabled or ThemeObjects.DeepESP.Enabled
			local isQODKillerESP = sharedESPEnabled and killerFolder and killerFolder:FindFirstChild(p.Name) ~= nil
			local isMurdererRoleESP = sharedESPEnabled and p == HubState.CurrentMurderer
			local isSheriffRoleESP = sharedESPEnabled and p == HubState.CurrentSheriff
			local roleColor = nil
			if isQODKillerESP or isMurdererRoleESP then
				roleColor = Color3.fromRGB(255, 70, 70)
			elseif isSheriffRoleESP then
				roleColor = Color3.fromRGB(70, 130, 255)
			end
			local showPlayerESP = sharedESPEnabled or roleColor ~= nil

			-- Infinite Yield-style body ESP. These adornments live under CoreGui
			-- instead of the character, so local transparency/hide effects used by
			-- games such as QOD do not erase the overlay for the killer.
			if ThemeObjects.DeepESP.Enabled and refreshESPBody then
				local adornments = ThemeObjects.ESPAdornments[p]
				if not adornments then
					adornments = {}
					ThemeObjects.ESPAdornments[p] = adornments
				end
				for part, adornment in pairs(adornments) do
					if not part.Parent or not part:IsDescendantOf(char) or not ThemeObjects.IsBodyESPPart(part, char) then
						if adornment then adornment:Destroy() end
						adornments[part] = nil
					end
				end
				for _, part in ipairs(char:GetChildren()) do
					if ThemeObjects.IsBodyESPPart(part, char) then
						local adornment = adornments[part]
						if not adornment then
							adornment = Instance.new("BoxHandleAdornment")
							adornment.Name = "PlayerESPPart"
							adornment.Adornee = part
							adornment.AlwaysOnTop = true
							adornment.ZIndex = 10
							adornment.Parent = ThemeObjects.ESPAdornmentRoot
							adornments[part] = adornment
						end
						adornment.Size = part.Size
						adornment.Color3 = roleColor or HubState.ESPColor
						adornment.Transparency = 0.64
					end
				end
			elseif not ThemeObjects.DeepESP.Enabled then
				ThemeObjects.ClearESPAdornments(p)
			end

			local oldCharacterHighlight = char:FindFirstChild("ESPHighlight")
			if oldCharacterHighlight then oldCharacterHighlight:Destroy() end
			local regularHighlight = ThemeObjects.ESPHighlights[p]
			if HubState.ESPEnabled then
				if not regularHighlight then
					regularHighlight = Instance.new("Highlight")
					regularHighlight.Name = "ESPHighlight"
					regularHighlight.Parent = ThemeObjects.ESPAdornmentRoot
					ThemeObjects.ESPHighlights[p] = regularHighlight
				end
				regularHighlight.Enabled = true
				regularHighlight.Adornee = char
				regularHighlight.DepthMode = Enum.HighlightDepthMode.AlwaysOnTop
				regularHighlight.FillColor = roleColor or HubState.ESPColor
				regularHighlight.FillTransparency = 0.72
				regularHighlight.OutlineColor = roleColor or HubState.ESPColor
				regularHighlight.OutlineTransparency = 0
			elseif regularHighlight then
				regularHighlight:Destroy()
				ThemeObjects.ESPHighlights[p] = nil
			end

			local head = char:FindFirstChild("Head")
			local labelPart = head or root
			if showPlayerESP and labelPart then
				if labelPart ~= head and head and head:FindFirstChild("ESPGui") then head.ESPGui:Destroy() end
				if labelPart ~= root and root and root:FindFirstChild("ESPGui") then root.ESPGui:Destroy() end
				local espGui = labelPart:FindFirstChild("ESPGui")
				if not espGui then
					espGui = Instance.new("BillboardGui", labelPart)
					espGui.Name = "ESPGui"
					espGui.Size = UDim2.new(0, 200, 0, 50)
					espGui.AlwaysOnTop = true
					espGui.StudsOffset = Vector3.new(0, 5, 0)
					local label = Instance.new("TextLabel", espGui)
					label.Name = "ESPLabel"
					label.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
					label.BackgroundTransparency = 1
					label.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
					label.TextSize = 12
					label.TextStrokeTransparency = 0
				end
				local dist = (RootPart and (RootPart.Position - root.Position).Magnitude) or 0
				espGui.ESPLabel.TextColor3 = roleColor or HubState.ESPColor
				espGui.ESPLabel.Text = string.format("%s\nHP: %d | %d Studs", p.DisplayName, math.floor(hum.Health), math.floor(dist))
			else
				if head and head:FindFirstChild("ESPGui") then head.ESPGui:Destroy() end
				if root and root:FindFirstChild("ESPGui") then root.ESPGui:Destroy() end
			end

        end
    end
end)

-- Main Toggle/Minimizing logic
HubState.settingsOpen = false
HubState.minimized = false

ThemeObjects.CloseTransientPopups = function()
	if ThemeObjects.PickerDock then ThemeObjects.PickerDock.Visible = false end
	if ThemeObjects.GuiSizeDock then ThemeObjects.GuiSizeDock.Visible = false end
	if ThemeObjects.KeybindEditorFrame then ThemeObjects.KeybindEditorFrame.Visible = false end
	if ThemeObjects.ConfirmClearFrame then ThemeObjects.ConfirmClearFrame.Visible = false end
	if ThemeObjects.KeybindEditorConnection then
		ThemeObjects.KeybindEditorConnection:Disconnect()
		ThemeObjects.KeybindEditorConnection = nil
	end
	HubState.IsBindingKeybindEditor = false
end

local function ToggleSettings(forceClose)
	HubState.settingsOpen = forceClose and false or not HubState.settingsOpen
	ThemeObjects.UpdateEmblemPosition()
	if not forceClose then PlayClick() end
	local posMove = HubState.settingsOpen and 1.1 or 0 
    local posSet = HubState.settingsOpen and 0 or 1.1
	local activeX = 114
	HubState.MovementPage:TweenPosition(UDim2.new(posMove, activeX, 0, 54), "Out", "Quart", 0.4, true)
	HubState.CombatPage:TweenPosition(UDim2.new(posMove, activeX, 0, 54), "Out", "Quart", 0.4, true)
	ThemeObjects.CameraPage:TweenPosition(UDim2.new(posMove, activeX, 0, 54), "Out", "Quart", 0.4, true)
	HubState.TeleportPage:TweenPosition(UDim2.new(posMove, activeX, 0, 54), "Out", "Quart", 0.4, true)
	HubState.GamesPage:TweenPosition(UDim2.new(posMove, activeX, 0, 54), "Out", "Quart", 0.4, true)
	HubState.MM2Page:TweenPosition(UDim2.new(posMove, activeX, 0, 54), "Out", "Quart", 0.4, true)
	local extrasPage = MainFrame:FindFirstChild("ExtrasPage")
	if extrasPage then extrasPage:TweenPosition(UDim2.new(posMove, activeX, 0, 54), "Out", "Quart", 0.4, true) end
	local quietPage = MainFrame:FindFirstChild("QuietOrDiePage")
	if quietPage then quietPage:TweenPosition(UDim2.new(posMove, activeX, 0, 54), "Out", "Quart", 0.4, true) end
	HubState.TabScroll.Visible = not HubState.minimized
	if not HubState.settingsOpen then
		ThemeObjects.CloseTransientPopups()
	end
	HubState.PageHeader:TweenPosition(UDim2.new(posMove, activeX, 0, 32), "Out", "Quart", 0.4, true)
	HubState.SettingsPage:TweenPosition(UDim2.new(posSet, activeX, 0, 32), "Out", "Quart", 0.4, true)
end
HubState.SettingsBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
	if HubState.minimized then return end
	ToggleSettings()
end)

local function ToggleGUI()
	HubState.minimized = not HubState.minimized
	PlayMinimizeSound(HubState.minimized)
	if HubState.minimized and HubState.settingsOpen then ToggleSettings(true) end
	if HubState.minimized and ThemeObjects.CloseTransientPopups then ThemeObjects.CloseTransientPopups() end
	HubState.TabScroll.Visible = not HubState.minimized
	HubState.PageHeader.Visible = not HubState.minimized
	ThemeObjects.UpdateEmblemPosition()
	if not HubState.minimized then HubState.SettingsBtn.Visible = true end
	HubState.SettingsBtn.Active = not HubState.minimized
	TweenService:Create(HubState.SettingsBtn, TweenInfo.new(0.2), {
		BackgroundTransparency = HubState.minimized and 1 or 0,
		TextTransparency = HubState.minimized and 1 or 0,
		TextStrokeTransparency = HubState.minimized and 1 or 0.5,
	}):Play()
	if HubState.minimized then
		task.delay(0.2, function()
			if HubState.minimized then HubState.SettingsBtn.Visible = false end
		end)
	end
	local targetSize = HubState.minimized and UDim2.new(0, 170, 0, 34) or UDim2.new(0, 460, 0, 300)
	TweenService:Create(MainFrame, TweenInfo.new(0.4, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {Size = targetSize}):Play()
	HubState.MiniButton.Text = HubState.minimized and "+" or "-"
end
HubState.MiniButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(ToggleGUI)

-- Input Listener
HubState.Connections.InputBegan = UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, processed)
	if processed or HubState.IsBindingSpeed or HubState.IsBindingFly or HubState.IsBindingNoclip or ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Binding or HubState.IsBindingAutoLock or HubState.IsBindingESP or HubState.IsBindingFlingMenu or ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.Binding or HubState.IsBindingKeybindEditor then return end
	if input.UserInputType ~= Enum.UserInputType.Keyboard then return end
	if ThemeObjects.RunFeatureKeybind and ThemeObjects.RunFeatureKeybind(input.KeyCode) then return
	elseif input.KeyCode == HubState.SpeedKeybind then ToggleSpeed()
	elseif input.KeyCode == HubState.FlyKeybind then ToggleFly()
	elseif input.KeyCode == HubState.NoclipKeybind then ToggleNoclip()
	elseif input.KeyCode == ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Keybind then ThemeObjects.FreeCam.ToggleState()
	elseif input.KeyCode == HubState.AutoLockKeybind then ToggleAutoLock()
	elseif input.KeyCode == HubState.ESPKeybind then ToggleESP()
	elseif input.KeyCode == HubState.FlingMenuKeybind then ToggleFlingMenu()
	elseif input.KeyCode == ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.Keybind then ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.Toggle()
    elseif input.KeyCode == HubState.MinimizeKeybind then ToggleGUI() 
    end
end)

-- Tab Setup
HubState.TabNames = {"Movement", "Combat", "Camera", "Teleport", "Games", "Extras"}
ThemeObjects.ActiveTabName = "Movement"
HubState.ActiveContentPage = HubState.MovementPage
HubState.ActiveTabIndex = 1
ThemeObjects.TabTransitionId = 0
ThemeObjects.SwitchTab = function(name)
	if HubState.settingsOpen then ToggleSettings(true) end
	if ThemeObjects.CloseTransientPopups then ThemeObjects.CloseTransientPopups() end
	local previousIndex = HubState.ActiveTabIndex or table.find(HubState.TabNames, ThemeObjects.ActiveTabName) or 1
	local nextIndex = table.find(HubState.TabNames, name) or previousIndex
	local direction = nextIndex >= previousIndex and 1 or -1
	local activeX = 114
	local activeY = 54
	local headerX = 120
	local headerY = 32
	local slideDistance = 18
	local headerSlideDistance = 18
	local slideTime = 0.18
	local slideTweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(slideTime, Enum.EasingStyle.Quint, Enum.EasingDirection.Out)
	local headerTweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(0.28, Enum.EasingStyle.Quint, Enum.EasingDirection.Out)
	local openingSelectedGame = name == "Games" and HubState.SelectedGame ~= nil
	local quietPage = MainFrame:FindFirstChild("QuietOrDiePage")
	local extrasPage = MainFrame:FindFirstChild("ExtrasPage")
	local incomingPage = HubState.MovementPage
	ThemeObjects.TabTransitionId += 1
	local transitionId = ThemeObjects.TabTransitionId
	local function setPageContentTransparency(page, value)
		if not page or not page.Parent then return end
		for _, object in ipairs(page:GetDescendants()) do
			if object:IsA("TextLabel") or object:IsA("TextButton") or object:IsA("TextBox") then
				object.TextTransparency = value
			elseif object:IsA("ImageLabel") or object:IsA("ImageButton") then
				object.ImageTransparency = value
			elseif object:IsA("UIStroke") then
				if object:GetAttribute("TransitionBaseStrokeTransparency") == nil then
					object:SetAttribute("TransitionBaseStrokeTransparency", object.Transparency)
				end
				local baseTransparency = object:GetAttribute("TransitionBaseStrokeTransparency") or 0
				object.Transparency = math.clamp(baseTransparency + value, 0, 1)
			end
			if object:IsA("GuiObject") and object.BackgroundTransparency < 1 then
				if object:GetAttribute("TransitionBaseBackgroundTransparency") == nil then
					object:SetAttribute("TransitionBaseBackgroundTransparency", object.BackgroundTransparency)
				end
				local baseTransparency = object:GetAttribute("TransitionBaseBackgroundTransparency") or 0
				object.BackgroundTransparency = math.clamp(baseTransparency + value, 0, 1)
			end
		end
	end
	local function restorePageContentTransparency(page)
		if not page or not page.Parent then return end
		for _, object in ipairs(page:GetDescendants()) do
			if object:IsA("TextLabel") or object:IsA("TextButton") or object:IsA("TextBox") then
				object.TextTransparency = 0
			elseif object:IsA("ImageLabel") or object:IsA("ImageButton") then
				object.ImageTransparency = 0
			elseif object:IsA("UIStroke") then
				local baseTransparency = object:GetAttribute("TransitionBaseStrokeTransparency")
				if baseTransparency ~= nil then
					object.Transparency = baseTransparency
					object:SetAttribute("TransitionBaseStrokeTransparency", nil)
				end
			end
			if object:IsA("GuiObject") then
				local baseTransparency = object:GetAttribute("TransitionBaseBackgroundTransparency")
				if baseTransparency ~= nil then
					object.BackgroundTransparency = baseTransparency
					object:SetAttribute("TransitionBaseBackgroundTransparency", nil)
				end
			end
		end
	end

	ThemeObjects.ActiveTabName = name
	HubState.ActiveTabIndex = nextIndex
	HubState.PageHeader.Text = openingSelectedGame and HubState.SelectedGame or name
	HubState.PageHeader.Position = UDim2.new(0, headerX, 0, headerY + (headerSlideDistance * direction))
	TweenService:Create(HubState.PageHeader, headerTweenInfo, {Position = UDim2.new(0, headerX, 0, headerY)}):Play()
	HubState.MM2BackButton.Visible = openingSelectedGame
	if HubState.GamesTabButton then
		HubState.GamesTabButton.Text = HubState.SelectedGame or "Games"
	end
	if HubState.TabScroll then
		for _, tabButton in ipairs(HubState.TabScroll:GetChildren()) do
			if tabButton:IsA("TextButton") then
				local selected = tabButton.Text == name or (tabButton == HubState.GamesTabButton and name == "Games")
				tabButton.TextColor3 = selected and AccentColor or Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
			end
		end
	end

	if name == "Teleport" and not ThemeObjects.PlayerListReady then UpdatePlayerList() end
	if name == "Movement" then incomingPage = HubState.MovementPage
	elseif name == "Combat" then incomingPage = HubState.CombatPage
	elseif name == "Camera" then incomingPage = ThemeObjects.CameraPage
	elseif name == "Teleport" then incomingPage = HubState.TeleportPage
	elseif name == "Extras" and extrasPage then incomingPage = extrasPage
	elseif name == "Games" and openingSelectedGame and HubState.SelectedGame == "MM2" then incomingPage = HubState.MM2Page
	elseif name == "Games" and openingSelectedGame and HubState.SelectedGame == "Quiet Or Die" and quietPage then incomingPage = quietPage
	elseif name == "Games" then incomingPage = HubState.GamesPage end

	if name == "Games" and openingSelectedGame and HubState.SelectedGame == "MM2" then
		if ThemeObjects.RefreshMM2RolesFromRemote then ThemeObjects.RefreshMM2RolesFromRemote() end
		if ThemeObjects.RefreshMM2RolesFromTools then ThemeObjects.RefreshMM2RolesFromTools() end
	end

	local quietCoins = HubState.PageHeader:FindFirstChild("QuietOrDieCoinsDisplay")
	if quietCoins then quietCoins.Visible = openingSelectedGame and HubState.SelectedGame == "Quiet Or Die" end
	local quietWins = HubState.PageHeader:FindFirstChild("QuietOrDieWinsDisplay")
	if quietWins then quietWins.Visible = openingSelectedGame and HubState.SelectedGame == "Quiet Or Die" end
	local quietHistory = HubState.PageHeader:FindFirstChild("QuietOrDieHistoryButton")
	if quietHistory then quietHistory.Visible = openingSelectedGame and HubState.SelectedGame == "Quiet Or Die" end
	if quietPage and not (openingSelectedGame and HubState.SelectedGame == "Quiet Or Die") then
		local historyPanel = quietPage:FindFirstChild("QuietOrDieHistoryPanel")
		if historyPanel then historyPanel.Visible = false end
	end

	local pages = {HubState.MovementPage, HubState.CombatPage, ThemeObjects.CameraPage, HubState.TeleportPage, HubState.GamesPage, HubState.MM2Page, extrasPage, quietPage}
	local outgoingPage = HubState.ActiveContentPage
	for _, page in ipairs(pages) do
		if page and page ~= incomingPage and page ~= outgoingPage then
			restorePageContentTransparency(page)
			page.Visible = false
			page.Position = UDim2.new(1.1, 0, 0, activeY)
		end
	end

	incomingPage.Visible = true
	if outgoingPage and outgoingPage ~= incomingPage and outgoingPage.Parent then
		restorePageContentTransparency(incomingPage)
		restorePageContentTransparency(outgoingPage)
		setPageContentTransparency(incomingPage, 1)
		incomingPage.Position = UDim2.new(0, activeX, 0, activeY + (slideDistance * direction))
		outgoingPage.Visible = true
		outgoingPage.Position = UDim2.new(0, activeX, 0, activeY)
		setPageContentTransparency(outgoingPage, 0.85)
		task.delay(0.035, function()
			if ThemeObjects.TabTransitionId == transitionId and outgoingPage and outgoingPage.Parent and outgoingPage ~= HubState.ActiveContentPage then
				outgoingPage.Visible = false
				outgoingPage.Position = UDim2.new(1.1, 0, 0, activeY)
				restorePageContentTransparency(outgoingPage)
			end
		end)
		task.spawn(function()
			local startedAt = os.clock()
			while ThemeObjects.TabTransitionId == transitionId and os.clock() - startedAt < slideTime do
				local alpha = math.clamp((os.clock() - startedAt) / slideTime, 0, 1)
				setPageContentTransparency(incomingPage, 1 - alpha)
				RunService.RenderStepped:Wait()
			end
			if ThemeObjects.TabTransitionId == transitionId then
				setPageContentTransparency(incomingPage, 0)
			end
		end)
		local incomingTween = TweenService:Create(incomingPage, slideTweenInfo, {Position = UDim2.new(0, activeX, 0, activeY)})
		incomingTween:Play()
	else
		restorePageContentTransparency(incomingPage)
		incomingPage.Position = UDim2.new(0, activeX, 0, activeY)
	end
	HubState.ActiveContentPage = incomingPage
	ThemeObjects.RefreshStateTexts(true)
	task.delay(slideTime + 0.04, function()
		if ThemeObjects.TabTransitionId == transitionId then
			restorePageContentTransparency(incomingPage)
			UpdateTheme(true)
		end
	end)
end
for i, name in ipairs(HubState.TabNames) do
	local TabBtn = Instance.new("TextButton")
	TabBtn.Name = "NavTabButton"
		TabBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0, 94, 0, 34)
	TabBtn.LayoutOrder = i
	TabBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(38, 38, 52)
	TabBtn.BackgroundTransparency = 0.8
	TabBtn.BorderSizePixel = 0
	TabBtn.Text = name
	TabBtn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
	TabBtn.TextSize = 11
	TabBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
	TabBtn.TextTransparency = 0
	TabBtn.Parent = HubState.TabScroll
	if name == "Games" then HubState.GamesTabButton = TabBtn end
	table.insert(ThemeObjects.Backgrounds, TabBtn)
	table.insert(ThemeObjects.Texts, TabBtn)
	Instance.new("UICorner", TabBtn).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)
	
	TabBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		PlayClick()
		ThemeObjects.SwitchTab(name)
	end)
end

ResetCharacterBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
	PlayClick()
	local character = Player.Character
	if character then character:BreakJoints() end
end)

RejoinBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
	PlayClick()
	if ThemeObjects.RejoinBusy then return end
	ThemeObjects.RejoinBusy = true
	task.spawn(function()
		local queueTeleport = queue_on_teleport
			or (type(syn) == "table" and syn.queue_on_teleport)
			or (type(fluxus) == "table" and fluxus.queue_on_teleport)
		if type(queueTeleport) ~= "function" then
			RejoinBtn.Text = "Queue Unsupported"
			task.wait(2)
			RejoinBtn.Text = "Rejoin"
			ThemeObjects.RejoinBusy = false
			return
		end
		for seconds = 5, 1, -1 do
			RejoinBtn.Text = "Saving... " .. seconds
			task.wait(1)
		end
		local queueCode = [[loadstring(game:HttpGet("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/hqydeuu-ux/Script-Hub/main/Script%20Hub?cache=" .. tostring(os.time())))()]]
		if not pcall(queueTeleport, queueCode) then
			RejoinBtn.Text = "Queue Failed"
			task.wait(2)
			RejoinBtn.Text = "Rejoin"
			ThemeObjects.RejoinBusy = false
			return
		end
		RejoinBtn.Text = "Rejoining..."
		local teleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
		local success = pcall(function()
			teleportService:TeleportToPlaceInstance(game.PlaceId, game.JobId, Player)
		end)
		if not success then
			RejoinBtn.Text = "Rejoin Failed"
			task.wait(2)
			RejoinBtn.Text = "Rejoin"
			ThemeObjects.RejoinBusy = false
		end
	end)
end)

ServerHopBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
	PlayClick()
	if ThemeObjects.ServerHopBusy then return end
	ThemeObjects.ServerHopBusy = true
	ServerHopBtn.Text = "Finding Server..."
	task.spawn(function()
		local availableServers = {}
		local cursor = nil
		local requestWorked = true
		for _ = 1, 5 do
			local url = "https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/" .. tostring(game.PlaceId)
				.. "/servers/Public?sortOrder=Asc&excludeFullGames=true&limit=100"
			if cursor and cursor ~= "" then
				url = url .. "&cursor=" .. HttpService:UrlEncode(cursor)
			end
			local success, response = pcall(function()
				return HttpService:JSONDecode(game:HttpGet(url))
			end)
			if not success or type(response) ~= "table" then
				requestWorked = false
				break
			end
			for _, server in ipairs(response.data or {}) do
				if server.id and server.id ~= game.JobId
					and tonumber(server.playing) and tonumber(server.maxPlayers)
					and server.playing < server.maxPlayers then
					table.insert(availableServers, server.id)
				end
			end
			cursor = response.nextPageCursor
			if not cursor or cursor == "" or #availableServers >= 100 then break end
		end

		if #availableServers == 0 then
			ServerHopBtn.Text = requestWorked and "No Servers Found" or "Server Search Failed"
			task.wait(2)
			ServerHopBtn.Text = "Server Hop"
			ThemeObjects.ServerHopBusy = false
			return
		end

		-- Directly selecting a public JobId bypasses Roblox's friend-preferred routing.
		local destination = availableServers[math.random(1, #availableServers)]
		ServerHopBtn.Text = "Joining New Server..."
		local success = pcall(function()
			game:GetService("TeleportService"):TeleportToPlaceInstance(game.PlaceId, destination, Player)
		end)
		if not success then
			ServerHopBtn.Text = "Teleport Failed"
			task.wait(2)
			ServerHopBtn.Text = "Server Hop"
			ThemeObjects.ServerHopBusy = false
		end
	end)
end)

local function ApplyGuiSize(value)
	GuiSizeValue = math.clamp(value, 20, 100)
	GuiSizeValueLabel.Text = tostring(GuiSizeValue)
	local targetScale = GuiScaleFromValue(GuiSizeValue)
	for _, scaleObject in ipairs({MainScaleObject, HubState.TargetScaleObject, ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.Scale, SplashScaleObject, ThemeObjects.PickerDockScale, ThemeObjects.GuiSizeDockScale, ThemeObjects.KeybindEditorScale, ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.CopyScale}) do
		if scaleObject and scaleObject.Parent then
			TweenService:Create(scaleObject, TweenInfo.new(0.2, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {Scale = targetScale}):Play()
		end
	end
	if ThemeObjects.UpdatePickerDockPosition then ThemeObjects.UpdatePickerDockPosition() end
	if ThemeObjects.UpdateGuiSizeDockPosition then ThemeObjects.UpdateGuiSizeDockPosition() end
	if ThemeObjects.UpdateKeybindEditorDockPosition then ThemeObjects.UpdateKeybindEditorDockPosition() end
	if ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.UpdateDockPosition then ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.UpdateDockPosition() end
	SavedKeybinds.GuiSize = GuiSizeValue
	SavePersistentSettings()
end

GuiSizeMinusBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() PlayClick() ApplyGuiSize(GuiSizeValue - 5) end)
GuiSizePlusBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() PlayClick() ApplyGuiSize(GuiSizeValue + 5) end)
GuiSizeResetBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() PlayClick() ApplyGuiSize(50) end)

local SavedColorButtons = {}

	local swatch = Instance.new("TextButton")

	swatch.BackgroundTransparency = 0.15

	swatch.Text = ""
	swatch.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
	swatch.TextSize = 10
	swatch.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
	swatch.ZIndex = 81
	swatch.Parent = PickerFrame
	table.insert(ThemeObjects.Backgrounds, swatch)
	Instance.new("UICorner", swatch).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4)
	local swatchStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
	swatchStroke.Name = "ControlOutline"
	swatchStroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
	swatchStroke.Thickness = 1
	swatchStroke.Transparency = 0
	swatchStroke.Parent = swatch
	SavedColorButtons[index] = swatch
end

	if pickerObject:IsA("GuiObject") then pickerObject.ZIndex = 81 end
end

ThemeObjects.KeybindEditorRows = {}
ThemeObjects.BuildKeybindEditorEntries = function()
	local entries = {
		{Name = "Minimize GUI", Storage = "MinimizeGUI", Get = function() return HubState.MinimizeKeybind end, Set = function(key)
			HubState.MinimizeKeybind = key
			SaveKeybind("MinimizeGUI", key)
		end, Action = ToggleGUI},
	}
	local featureEntries = {}
	for _, entry in ipairs(ThemeObjects.FeatureKeybindEntries) do
		table.insert(featureEntries, entry)
	end
	table.sort(featureEntries, function(a, b)
		return tostring(a.Name):lower() < tostring(b.Name):lower()
	end)
	for _, entry in ipairs(featureEntries) do
		table.insert(entries, entry)
	end
	return entries
end

ThemeObjects.RunFeatureKeybind = function(keyCode)
	if keyCode == Enum.KeyCode.Unknown then return false end
	local ranAny = false
	for _, entry in ipairs(ThemeObjects.BuildKeybindEditorEntries()) do
		if entry.Action and entry.Get and entry.Get() == keyCode then
			ranAny = true
			pcall(entry.Action)
		end
	end
	return ranAny
end

ThemeObjects.RefreshKeybindEditor = function()
	for _, row in ipairs(ThemeObjects.KeybindEditorRows) do
		if row.Row then row.Row:Destroy() end
	end
	ThemeObjects.KeybindEditorRows = {}
	ThemeObjects.KeybindEditorEntries = ThemeObjects.BuildKeybindEditorEntries()
	for index, entry in ipairs(ThemeObjects.KeybindEditorEntries) do
		local row = Instance.new("Frame")
		row.Name = "KeybindEditorRow"
		row.Size = UDim2.new(1, -8, 0, 28)
		row.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(65, 65, 67)
		row.BackgroundTransparency = 0.92
		row.BorderSizePixel = 0
		row.LayoutOrder = index
		row.ZIndex = 91
		row.Parent = KeybindEditorScroll
		table.insert(ThemeObjects.Backgrounds, row)
		Instance.new("UICorner", row).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)
		local rowStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
		rowStroke.Name = "ControlOutline"
		rowStroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
		rowStroke.Thickness = 1
		rowStroke.Transparency = 0.18
		rowStroke.Parent = row

		local label = Instance.new("TextLabel")
		label.Size = UDim2.new(1, -62, 1, 0)
		label.Position = UDim2.new(0, 8, 0, 0)
		label.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		label.Text = entry.Name
		label.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
		label.TextSize = 9
		label.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
		label.TextStrokeColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
		label.TextStrokeTransparency = 0.5
		label.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
		label.ZIndex = 92
		label.Parent = row
		table.insert(ThemeObjects.Texts, label)

		local button = Instance.new("TextButton")
		button.Size = UDim2.new(0, 46, 0, 20)
		button.Position = UDim2.new(1, -52, 0.5, -10)
		button.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(45, 45, 45)
		button.BackgroundTransparency = 0.8
		button.BorderSizePixel = 0
		button.Text = KeybindText(entry.Get())
		button.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
		button.TextSize = 8
		button.TextColor3 = AccentColor
		button.ZIndex = 92
		button.Parent = row
		table.insert(ThemeObjects.Backgrounds, button)
		table.insert(ThemeObjects.Accents, button)
		Instance.new("UICorner", button).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 5)
		local buttonStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
		buttonStroke.Name = "ControlOutline"
		buttonStroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
		buttonStroke.Thickness = 1
		buttonStroke.Transparency = 0
		buttonStroke.Parent = button
		table.insert(ThemeObjects.KeybindEditorRows, {Entry = entry, Button = button, Row = row})
		if entry.InlineButton then entry.InlineButton.Text = KeybindText(entry.Get()) end
		button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			ThemeObjects.BeginFeatureKeybind(entry, button)
		end)
		ThemeObjects.AttachKeybindClearPrompt(entry, button)
	end
	KeybindEditorScroll.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, math.max(KeybindEditorLayout.AbsoluteContentSize.Y + 6, #ThemeObjects.KeybindEditorRows * 32))
end
ThemeObjects.RefreshKeybindEditor()

local PickerTarget = "Accent"
local PickerH, PickerS, PickerV = 0, 0, 1
local DraggingSV = false
local DraggingHue = false

local function RefreshThemePreviews()
	AccentColorBtn.BackgroundColor3 = AccentColor
	AccentColorBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
	if HubState.ESPColorBtn then
		HubState.ESPColorBtn.BackgroundColor3 = HubState.ESPColor
		HubState.ESPColorBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
	end
end

local function RefreshPickerMarkers()
	SVWheel.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromHSV(PickerH, 1, 1)
	SVMarker.Position = UDim2.new(PickerS, 0, 1 - PickerV, 0)
	HueMarker.Position = UDim2.new(0, -2, PickerH, -1)
end

local function PickerPaletteKey()
	return PickerTarget == "ESP" and "PlayerESPSavedColors" or "AccentSavedColors"
end

local function PickerCurrentColor()
	return PickerTarget == "ESP" and HubState.ESPColor or AccentColor
end

local function SaveESPColor()
	SavedKeybinds.PlayerESPColor = PackColor(HubState.ESPColor)
	SavePersistentSettings()
end

local function RefreshSavedColorButtons()
	local savedColors = type(SavedKeybinds[PickerPaletteKey()]) == "table" and SavedKeybinds[PickerPaletteKey()] or {}
	for index, swatch in ipairs(SavedColorButtons) do
		local color = UnpackColor(savedColors[index], Color3.fromRGB(45, 45, 45))
		swatch.BackgroundColor3 = color
		swatch.Text = savedColors[index] and "" or "+"
	end
end

local function ApplyPickerColor()
	local selectedColor = Color3.fromHSV(PickerH, PickerS, PickerV)
	if PickerTarget == "ESP" then
		HubState.ESPColor = selectedColor
		SaveESPColor()
	else
		AccentColor = selectedColor
	end
	RefreshThemePreviews()
	RefreshPickerMarkers()
	UpdateTheme(true)
	if PickerTarget == "Accent" and (not ThemeObjects.LastPickerSave or os.clock() - ThemeObjects.LastPickerSave > 0.15) then
		ThemeObjects.LastPickerSave = os.clock()
		SaveThemeColors()
	end
end

local function OpenColorPicker(target)
	PickerTarget = target == "ESP" and "ESP" or "Accent"
	GuiSizeFrame.Visible = false
	if KeybindEditorFrame then KeybindEditorFrame.Visible = false end
	if ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.CopyFrame and ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.CopyFrame.Visible then
		ThemeObjects.ExtrasFeature.EndSelection(true)
	end
	local selectedColor = PickerCurrentColor()
	PickerH, PickerS, PickerV = Color3.toHSV(selectedColor)
	ConfirmClearFrame.Visible = false
	PickerFrame.Visible = true
	ResetThemeBtn.Visible = PickerTarget == "Accent"
	SaveCurrentColorBtn.Visible = true
	RefreshPickerMarkers()
	RefreshSavedColorButtons()
end

SaveCurrentColorBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
	PlayClick()
	local key = PickerPaletteKey()
	local savedColors = type(SavedKeybinds[key]) == "table" and SavedKeybinds[key] or {}
	table.insert(savedColors, 1, PackColor(PickerCurrentColor()))
	while #savedColors > 5 do table.remove(savedColors) end
	SavedKeybinds[key] = savedColors
	SavePersistentSettings()
	RefreshSavedColorButtons()
end)

for index, swatch in ipairs(SavedColorButtons) do
	swatch.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		PlayClick()
		local savedColors = type(SavedKeybinds[PickerPaletteKey()]) == "table" and SavedKeybinds[PickerPaletteKey()] or {}
		local color = UnpackColor(savedColors[index], nil)
		if not color then return end
		PickerH, PickerS, PickerV = Color3.toHSV(color)
		ApplyPickerColor()
		RefreshSavedColorButtons()
	end)
end

local function UpdateSVFromPosition(position)
	local x = math.clamp((position.X - SVInput.AbsolutePosition.X) / SVInput.AbsoluteSize.X, 0, 1)
	local y = math.clamp((position.Y - SVInput.AbsolutePosition.Y) / SVInput.AbsoluteSize.Y, 0, 1)
	PickerS = x
	PickerV = 1 - y
	ApplyPickerColor()
end

local function UpdateHueFromPosition(position)
	PickerH = math.clamp((position.Y - HueInput.AbsolutePosition.Y) / HueInput.AbsoluteSize.Y, 0, 1)
	ApplyPickerColor()
end

SVInput.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
	if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
		DraggingSV = true
		UpdateSVFromPosition(input.Position)
	end
end)
HueInput.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
	if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
		DraggingHue = true
		UpdateHueFromPosition(input.Position)
	end
end)
TrackConnection("PickerInputChanged", UserInputService.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
	if DraggingSV and (input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch) then
		UpdateSVFromPosition(input.Position)
	elseif DraggingHue and (input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch) then
		UpdateHueFromPosition(input.Position)
	end
end))
TrackConnection("PickerInputEnded", UserInputService.InputEnded:Connect(function(input)
	if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
		if DraggingSV or DraggingHue then SaveThemeColors() end
		DraggingSV = false
		DraggingHue = false
	end
end))

AccentColorBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
	PlayClick()
	GuiSizeFrame.Visible = false
	if KeybindEditorFrame then KeybindEditorFrame.Visible = false end
	if PickerFrame.Visible and PickerTarget == "Accent" then
		PickerFrame.Visible = false
		ResetThemeBtn.Visible = false
		SaveCurrentColorBtn.Visible = false
	else
		OpenColorPicker("Accent")
	end
end)

if HubState.ESPColorBtn then
	HubState.ESPColorBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		PlayClick()
		GuiSizeFrame.Visible = false
		if KeybindEditorFrame then KeybindEditorFrame.Visible = false end
		if PickerFrame.Visible and PickerTarget == "ESP" then
			PickerFrame.Visible = false
			SaveCurrentColorBtn.Visible = false
		else
			OpenColorPicker("ESP")
		end
	end)
end

GuiSizeBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
	PlayClick()
	local willOpen = not GuiSizeFrame.Visible
	PickerFrame.Visible = false
	ResetThemeBtn.Visible = false
	if SaveCurrentColorBtn then SaveCurrentColorBtn.Visible = false end
	ConfirmClearFrame.Visible = false
	if KeybindEditorFrame then KeybindEditorFrame.Visible = false end
	GuiSizeFrame.Visible = willOpen
	if willOpen and ThemeObjects.UpdateGuiSizeDockPosition then
		ThemeObjects.UpdateGuiSizeDockPosition()
	end
end)
ResetThemeBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
	PlayClick()
	AccentColor = DefaultAccentColor
	SaveThemeColors()
	RefreshThemePreviews()
	UpdateTheme()
	if PickerFrame.Visible then OpenColorPicker(PickerTarget) end
end)

ClearKeybindsBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
	PlayClick()
	PickerFrame.Visible = false
	GuiSizeFrame.Visible = false
	ResetThemeBtn.Visible = false
	if SaveCurrentColorBtn then SaveCurrentColorBtn.Visible = false end
	if KeybindEditorFrame then KeybindEditorFrame.Visible = false end
	ConfirmClearFrame.Visible = true
end)
ConfirmNoBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() PlayClick() ConfirmClearFrame.Visible = false end)
ConfirmYesBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
	PlayClick()
	HubState.SpeedKeybind = Enum.KeyCode.Unknown
	HubState.FlyKeybind = Enum.KeyCode.Unknown
	HubState.NoclipKeybind = Enum.KeyCode.Unknown
	ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Keybind = Enum.KeyCode.Unknown
	HubState.AutoLockKeybind = Enum.KeyCode.Unknown
	HubState.ESPKeybind = Enum.KeyCode.Unknown
	HubState.FlingMenuKeybind = Enum.KeyCode.Unknown
	ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.Keybind = Enum.KeyCode.Unknown
	SavedKeybinds.Speed = "Unknown"
	SavedKeybinds.Fly = "Unknown"
	SavedKeybinds.Noclip = "Unknown"
	SavedKeybinds.FreeCam = "Unknown"
	SavedKeybinds.AutoLock = "Unknown"
	SavedKeybinds.ESP = "Unknown"
	SavedKeybinds.FlingMenu = "Unknown"
	SavedKeybinds.PlayerTPMenu = "Unknown"
	HubState.SpeedBindBtn.Text = "..."
	HubState.FlyBindBtn.Text = "..."
	HubState.NoclipBindBtn.Text = "..."
	ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Bind.Text = "..."
	HubState.AutoLockBindBtn.Text = "..."
	HubState.ESPBindBtn.Text = "..."
	HubState.FlingBindBtn.Text = "..."
	if ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.BindButton then ThemeObjects.PlayerTP.BindButton.Text = "..." end
	if ThemeObjects.BuildKeybindEditorEntries then
		for _, entry in ipairs(ThemeObjects.BuildKeybindEditorEntries()) do
			if entry.Set then entry.Set(Enum.KeyCode.Unknown) end
			if entry.Button and entry.Button.Parent then entry.Button.Text = "..." end
			if entry.InlineButton and entry.InlineButton.Parent then entry.InlineButton.Text = "..." end
		end
	end
	if ThemeObjects.RefreshKeybindEditor then ThemeObjects.RefreshKeybindEditor() end
	if ThemeObjects.KeybindClearPrompt then ThemeObjects.KeybindClearPrompt:Destroy(); ThemeObjects.KeybindClearPrompt = nil end
	SavePersistentSettings()
	ConfirmClearFrame.Visible = false
end)

RefreshThemePreviews()
end
BuildSettingsPage()

local function Cleanup()
	if ThemeObjects.FreeCam and ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Enabled then ThemeObjects.FreeCam.Disable() end
	if ThemeObjects.ClearESPAdornments then ThemeObjects.ClearESPAdornments() end
	RestoreAntiFlingCollisions()
	RestoreKillHitboxes()
	HubState.GunDropESP.Clear()
	if ThemeObjects.CleanupPartSelector then ThemeObjects.CleanupPartSelector() end
	if ThemeObjects.FlushQuietHistory then ThemeObjects.FlushQuietHistory() end
	if ThemeObjects.RestoreFullBright then ThemeObjects.RestoreFullBright() end
	if ThemeObjects.RestoreQuietClutter then ThemeObjects.RestoreQuietClutter() end
	local Character = Player.Character
	if Character then
		local Hum = Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") local Root = Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
		if Hum then Hum.WalkSpeed = 16 end
		if Root then 
			Root.Velocity = Vector3.new(0,0,0) 
			if Root:FindFirstChildOfClass("BodyVelocity") then Root:FindFirstChildOfClass("BodyVelocity"):Destroy() end
			if Root:FindFirstChildOfClass("BodyGyro") then Root:FindFirstChildOfClass("BodyGyro"):Destroy() end
		end
		for _, part in pairs(Character:GetDescendants()) do if part:IsA("BasePart") then part.CanCollide = true end end
	end
	for _, p in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
		local cleanupCharacter = ThemeObjects.ResolveESPCharacter and ThemeObjects.ResolveESPCharacter(p) or p.Character
		if cleanupCharacter then
			if cleanupCharacter:FindFirstChild("ESPHighlight") then cleanupCharacter.ESPHighlight:Destroy() end
			if cleanupCharacter:FindFirstChild("MurdererRoleHighlight") then cleanupCharacter.MurdererRoleHighlight:Destroy() end
			if cleanupCharacter:FindFirstChild("SheriffRoleHighlight") then cleanupCharacter.SheriffRoleHighlight:Destroy() end
			if cleanupCharacter:FindFirstChild("Head") and cleanupCharacter.Head:FindFirstChild("ESPGui") then cleanupCharacter.Head.ESPGui:Destroy() end
			local cleanupRoot = cleanupCharacter:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or cleanupCharacter:FindFirstChild("UpperTorso") or cleanupCharacter:FindFirstChild("Torso") or cleanupCharacter.PrimaryPart
			if cleanupRoot and cleanupRoot:FindFirstChild("ESPGui") then cleanupRoot.ESPGui:Destroy() end
		end
	end
	for _, connection in pairs(HubState.Connections) do if connection then connection:Disconnect() end end
	if HubState.CoinFarmConnection then HubState.CoinFarmConnection:Disconnect() end
	ScreenGui:Destroy()
end
HubState.DestroyBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(Cleanup)

-- Keep feature tiles in the same translucent style as the Camera page.
for _, surface in ipairs(MainFrame:GetDescendants()) do
	if surface:IsA("Frame") and surface.BackgroundTransparency < 0.9 then
		local name = surface.Name
		if name:find("Card", 1, true) or name:find("Row", 1, true) then
			surface.BackgroundTransparency = 0.92
		end
	end
end

CompactGuiText(ScreenGui)
for _, entry in ipairs(ThemeObjects.FeatureKeybindEntries) do
	if entry.Button then ThemeObjects.EnsureKeybindOutline(entry.Button) end
	if entry.InlineButton then ThemeObjects.EnsureKeybindOutline(entry.InlineButton) end
end
UpdateTheme()

-- Dragging
HubState.dragging = nil
HubState.dragStart = nil
HubState.startPos = nil
TrackConnection("MainFrameDragStart", MainFrame.InputBegan:Connect(function(input) if (input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch) then HubState.dragging = true HubState.dragStart = input.Position HubState.startPos = MainFrame.Position input.Changed:Connect(function() if input.UserInputState == Enum.UserInputState.End then HubState.dragging = false end end) end end))
TrackConnection("MainFrameDragMove", UserInputService.InputChanged:Connect(function(input) if HubState.dragging and (input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch) then local delta = input.Position - HubState.dragStart MainFrame.Position = UDim2.new(HubState.startPos.X.Scale, HubState.startPos.X.Offset + delta.X, HubState.startPos.Y.Scale, HubState.startPos.Y.Offset + delta.Y) end end))

-- FLY-IN TITLE SEQUENCE
task.spawn(function()
	SplashFrame.Rotation = -540
	local spinIn = TweenService:Create(SplashFrame, TweenInfo.new(0.55, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {
		Size = UDim2.new(0, 200, 0, 200),
		Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.5, 0),
		Rotation = 0,
	})
	spinIn:Play()
	spinIn.Completed:Wait()

	local revealTitle = TweenService:Create(SplashText, TweenInfo.new(0.2, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {
		TextTransparency = 0,
		TextStrokeTransparency = 0.5,
	})
	revealTitle:Play()
	revealTitle.Completed:Wait()
	task.wait(0.5)

	local splashStroke = SplashFrame:FindFirstChildOfClass("UIStroke")
	if splashStroke then
		TweenService:Create(splashStroke, TweenInfo.new(0.4), {Transparency = 1}):Play()
	end
	TweenService:Create(SplashText, TweenInfo.new(0.25), {TextTransparency = 1, TextStrokeTransparency = 1}):Play()
	local spinOut = TweenService:Create(SplashFrame, TweenInfo.new(0.4, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.In), {
		Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0),
		Rotation = 540,
		BackgroundTransparency = 1,
	})
	spinOut:Play()
	spinOut.Completed:Wait()
	SplashFrame:Destroy()
	MainFrame.Visible = true
end)
